<script>
// ============================================
// ✅ XSS FIX: escapeHtml utility — server data ko kabhi bhi directly innerHTML mein mat daalo
// Yeh function sab dangerous characters ko safe HTML entities mein convert karta hai
// ============================================
function escapeHtml(str) {
  if (str === null || str === undefined) return '';
  return String(str)
    .replace(/&/g,  '&amp;')
    .replace(/</g,  '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g,  '&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g,  '&quot;')
    .replace(/'/g,  '&#x27;');
}

// ============================================
// GLOBAL VARIABLES
// ============================================
let currentUserId = '';
// ✅ FIX M-1: currentUserPassword global variable hataya — plain-text memory exposure fix
// Password ab sirf changePassword() ke local scope mein rahega
let currentUserData = {};
let currentUserToken = '';
let currentUserRole = '';

// ── Login screen live date/time clock ────────────────────────────
(function _loginClock() {
  var DAYS = ['Sunday','Monday','Tuesday','Wednesday','Thursday','Friday','Saturday'];
  var MONS = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];
  function tick() {
    var n = new Date();
    var d  = document.getElementById('lcDay');
    var dt = document.getElementById('lcDate');
    var t  = document.getElementById('lcTime');
    if (d)  d.textContent  = DAYS[n.getDay()];
    if (dt) dt.textContent = String(n.getDate()).padStart(2,'0') + ' ' + MONS[n.getMonth()] + ' ' + n.getFullYear();
    if (t)  t.textContent  = String(n.getHours()).padStart(2,'0') + ':' + String(n.getMinutes()).padStart(2,'0') + ':' + String(n.getSeconds()).padStart(2,'0');
  }
  tick();
  setInterval(tick, 1000);
})();

// ✅ FIX #3: Day management cache
let dayStartedCache = false;
let dayBranchCache = '';

// ✅ FIX #7: Auto-refresh interval
let walletRefreshInterval = null;

// ============================================
// UTILITY FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function showError(id, msg) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) {
    el.textContent = msg;
    el.style.display = 'block';
  }
}

function hideError(id) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) el.style.display = 'none';
}

function toggleSidebar() {
  const sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
  const overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
  sidebar.classList.toggle('open');
  overlay.classList.toggle('show');
}

function toggleOperatorSidebar() {
  const sidebar = document.getElementById('operatorSidebar');
  const overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
  sidebar.classList.toggle('open');
  overlay.classList.toggle('show');
}

function toggleSupervisorSidebar() {
  const sidebar = document.getElementById('supervisorSidebar');
  const overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
  sidebar.classList.toggle('open');
  overlay.classList.toggle('show');
}

function closeSidebar() {
  document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.remove('open');
  document.getElementById('operatorSidebar').classList.remove('open');
  document.getElementById('supervisorSidebar').classList.remove('open');
  document.getElementById('overlay').classList.remove('show');
}

// ============================================
// LOGIN TYPE SWITCHER
// ============================================
function switchLoginType(type) {
  const tabs = document.querySelectorAll('.login-tab');
  tabs.forEach(tab => {
    tab.classList.remove('active');
    if ((type === 'member' && tab.textContent.includes('Member')) ||
        (type === 'operator' && tab.textContent.includes('Operator')) ||
        (type === 'supervisor' && tab.textContent.includes('Supervisor'))) {
      tab.classList.add('active');
    }
  });
  
  document.getElementById('memberLoginForm').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('operatorLoginForm').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('supervisorLoginForm').classList.add('hidden');
  
  if (type === 'member') {
    document.getElementById('memberLoginForm').classList.remove('hidden');
  } else if (type === 'operator') {
    document.getElementById('operatorLoginForm').classList.remove('hidden');
  } else if (type === 'supervisor') {
    document.getElementById('supervisorLoginForm').classList.remove('hidden');
  }
}

// ============================================
// MEMBER LOGIN
// ============================================
function attemptLogin() {
  const uid = document.getElementById("userId").value.trim();
  const pwd = document.getElementById("password").value.trim();
  const btn = document.getElementById("loginBtn");
  
  hideError("loginError");
  
  if (!uid || !pwd) {
    showError("loginError", "Enter User ID and Password");
    return;
  }
  
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = "Logging in...";
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = "Login";
      
      if (res.success) {
        currentUserId = res.userId;
        // ✅ FIX M-1: Password memory mein store nahi karte
        currentUserToken = res.token;
        currentUserRole = 'MEMBER';
        
        // ✅ Store branchCode for request submission
        if (res.branchCode) {
          sessionStorage.setItem('memberBranchCode', res.branchCode);
        }
        
        document.getElementById("loginBox").style.display = "none";
        document.getElementById("dashboard").style.display = "block";
        loadUserData(res.userId);
        loadAnnouncements();
        
        checkNotificationsAfterLogin();
      } else {
        showError("loginError", res.message || "Login failed");
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = "Login";
      showError("loginError", "Error: " + err.message);
    })
    .login(uid, pwd);
}

// ============================================
// OPERATOR LOGIN
// ============================================
function attemptOperatorLogin() {
  const uid = document.getElementById('operatorUserId').value.trim();
  const pwd = document.getElementById('operatorPassword').value.trim();
  const btn = document.getElementById('operatorLoginBtn');
  const errDiv = document.getElementById('operatorLoginError');
  
  errDiv.style.display = 'none';
  
  if (!uid || !pwd) {
    errDiv.textContent = 'Enter credentials';
    errDiv.style.display = 'block';
    return;
  }
  
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = 'Logging in...';
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'Operator Login';
      
      if (res.success && res.role === 'OPERATOR') {
        currentUserId    = res.userId;
currentUserToken = res.token;
currentUserRole  = 'OPERATOR';

// ✅ FIX: sessionStorage mein bhi save karo (backup)
sessionStorage.setItem('operatorId',    res.userId);
sessionStorage.setItem('operatorToken', res.token);
sessionStorage.setItem('branchCode',    res.branchCode || '');
        
        document.getElementById('loginBox').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('operatorDashboard').classList.remove('hidden');
        document.getElementById('operatorNameDisplay').textContent = res.name || 'Operator';
        document.getElementById('operatorSidebarName').textContent = res.name || 'Operator';
        // ✅ Holiday warning — non-blocking, sirf alert
        if (res.isHoliday && res.holidayWarning) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            var banner = document.createElement('div');
            banner.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:20px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);' +
              'background:#e67e22;color:white;padding:16px 28px;border-radius:12px;' +
              'z-index:9999;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;' +
              'box-shadow:0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.4);max-width:90vw;line-height:1.6;';
            banner.innerHTML = res.holidayWarning.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
            var closeBtn = document.createElement('div');
            closeBtn.innerHTML = '✕';
            closeBtn.style.cssText = 'display:inline-block;margin-left:16px;cursor:pointer;font-size:18px;vertical-align:middle;opacity:0.8;';
            closeBtn.onclick = function() { banner.remove(); };
            banner.appendChild(closeBtn);
            document.body.appendChild(banner);
            setTimeout(function() { if (banner.parentElement) banner.remove(); }, 8000);
          }, 600);
        }

        
        loadOperatorData();
        loadOperatorDetailsNew(); // ✅ FIX #1: Load branch & wallet
        loadStaffAnnouncements('OPERATOR', 'operatorAnnouncementSection');
        
        startWalletAutoRefresh(); // ✅ FIX #7: Start auto-refresh
      } else {
        errDiv.textContent = res.message || 'Login failed';
        errDiv.style.display = 'block';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'Operator Login';
      errDiv.textContent = 'Error: ' + err.message;
      errDiv.style.display = 'block';
    })
    .operatorLogin(uid, pwd);
}

// ============================================
// SUPERVISOR LOGIN
// ============================================
function attemptSupervisorLogin() {
  const uid = document.getElementById('supervisorUserId').value.trim();
  const pwd = document.getElementById('supervisorPassword').value.trim();
  const btn = document.getElementById('supervisorLoginBtn');
  const errDiv = document.getElementById('supervisorLoginError');
  
  errDiv.style.display = 'none';
  
  if (!uid || !pwd) {
    errDiv.textContent = 'Enter credentials';
    errDiv.style.display = 'block';
    return;
  }
  
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = 'Logging in...';
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'Supervisor Login';
      
     if (res.success && res.role === 'SUPERVISOR') {
  // ✅ Set global variables
  currentUserId = res.userId;
  currentUserToken = res.token;
  currentUserRole = 'SUPERVISOR';
  
  console.log('✅ Login successful - Setting session:', res.userId);
  
  // ✅ CRITICAL: Store in sessionStorage for persistence across function calls
  sessionStorage.setItem('currentUserId', res.userId);
  sessionStorage.setItem('supervisorId', res.userId);
  sessionStorage.setItem('currentUserRole', 'SUPERVISOR');
  
  if (res.branchCode) {
    sessionStorage.setItem('branchCode', res.branchCode);
  }
  if (res.branchname) {
    sessionStorage.setItem('branchname', res.branchname);
  }
  if (res.dayStatus) {
    sessionStorage.setItem('dayStatus', res.dayStatus);
  }
  // ✅ FEATURE 1: Store previous day info
  if (res.isPreviousDay || res.branchPreviousDay) {
    sessionStorage.setItem('isPreviousDay', 'true');
    sessionStorage.setItem('openDayDate', res.openDayDate || '');
  } else {
    sessionStorage.removeItem('isPreviousDay');
    sessionStorage.removeItem('openDayDate');
  }

  // FIX: If mustCloseFirst, restrict operator menu immediately on login
  if (res.mustCloseFirst) {
    // Set state immediately — don't wait for 30sec refresh
    setTimeout(function() {
      setOperatorButtonState('PREV_DAY_OPEN');
      // Show banner
      var dash = document.getElementById('operatorDashboard') ||
                 document.querySelector('.operator-main') ||
                 document.body;
      if (dash && !document.getElementById('prevDayCounterBanner')) {
        var banner = document.createElement('div');
        banner.id = 'prevDayCounterBanner';
        banner.style.cssText =
          'background:#e67e22;color:white;padding:14px 20px;text-align:center;' +
          'font-weight:bold;font-size:14px;border-radius:10px;margin:10px 0;';
        banner.innerHTML =
          '⚠️ Pichle din ka Counter abhi bhi OPEN hai! (' + escapeHtml(res.openDayDate || '') + ')<br>' + // ✅ XSS fix
          '<span style="font-size:12px;font-weight:normal;">Koi bhi entry add nahi kar sakte jab tak counter close na ho.' +
          ' Neeche "Close Counter" button use karo.</span>';
        dash.insertBefore(banner, dash.firstChild);
      }
    }, 500);
  }

        document.getElementById('loginBox').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('supervisorDashboard').classList.remove('hidden');
        document.getElementById('supervisorNameDisplay').textContent = res.name || 'Supervisor';
        document.getElementById('supervisorSidebarName').textContent = res.name || 'Supervisor';
        // ✅ Holiday warning — non-blocking, sirf alert
        if (res.isHoliday && res.holidayWarning) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            var banner = document.createElement('div');
            banner.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:20px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);' +
              'background:#e67e22;color:white;padding:16px 28px;border-radius:12px;' +
              'z-index:9999;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;' +
              'box-shadow:0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.4);max-width:90vw;line-height:1.6;';
            banner.innerHTML = res.holidayWarning.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
            var closeBtn = document.createElement('div');
            closeBtn.innerHTML = '✕';
            closeBtn.style.cssText = 'display:inline-block;margin-left:16px;cursor:pointer;font-size:18px;vertical-align:middle;opacity:0.8;';
            closeBtn.onclick = function() { banner.remove(); };
            banner.appendChild(closeBtn);
            document.body.appendChild(banner);
            setTimeout(function() { if (banner.parentElement) banner.remove(); }, 8000);
          }, 600);
        }


        if (res.dayStatus) {
          updateDayStatusUI(res.dayStatus);
        }

        // ✅ FEATURE 1: Show previous day alert if needed
        if (res.mustCloseFirst && res.isPreviousDay) {
          showPreviousDayAlert(res.openDayDate);
          // FIX: Also immediately restrict menu — don't wait for live refresh
          setSupervisorPreviousDayMode(res.openDayDate);
        }

        loadSupervisorData();
        loadSupervisorDetailsNew();
        loadStaffAnnouncements('SUPERVISOR', 'supervisorAnnouncementSection');
        startWalletAutoRefresh();
      } else {
        errDiv.textContent = res.message || 'Login failed';
        errDiv.style.display = 'block';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'Supervisor Login';
      errDiv.textContent = 'Error: ' + err.message;
      errDiv.style.display = 'block';
    })
    .supervisorLogin(uid, pwd);
}

// ============================================
// ✅ FIX #1: LOAD OPERATOR DETAILS WITH BRANCH & WALLET
// ============================================
function loadOperatorDetailsNew() {
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result.success) {
        document.getElementById('opUserIdDisplay').textContent = result.userId || currentUserId;
        document.getElementById('opBranchCodeDisplay').textContent = result.branchCode || '-';
        document.getElementById('opBranchNameDisplay').textContent = result.branchName || result.branchCode || '-';
        
        dayBranchCache = result.branchCode; // ✅ Cache branch
        
   // Load wallet with retry
setTimeout(function() {
  loadOperatorWalletWithRetry();
}, 300);
// Load pending cash count
setTimeout(function() {
  loadPendingCashCount();
}, 500);
        loadOperatorCounterStatus();
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      console.error('Load operator details error:', error);
    })
    .getOperatorDetails(currentUserId);
}
function loadOperatorWallet() {
  console.log('Loading operator wallet for:', currentUserId);
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      console.log('Operator wallet result:', result);
      
      const walletDisplay = document.getElementById('opWalletDisplay');
      
      if (!walletDisplay) {
        console.error('Operator wallet display element not found');
        return;
      }
      
      if (result && result.success) {
        const balance = result.balance || 0;
        walletDisplay.textContent = '₹' + balance.toFixed(2);
        console.log('✅ Operator wallet balance set to:', balance);
      } else {
        walletDisplay.textContent = '₹0.00';
        console.warn('Operator wallet load failed:', result);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      console.error('Load operator wallet error:', error);
      const walletDisplay = document.getElementById('opWalletDisplay');
      if (walletDisplay) {
        walletDisplay.textContent = '₹0.00';
      }
    })
    .getOperatorWalletBalance(currentUserId);
}
// Get operator wallet balance with retry
function getOperatorWalletBalance() {
  console.log('Getting operator wallet balance for:', currentUserId);
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      console.log('Operator wallet info:', result);
      
      const walletDisplay = document.getElementById('opWalletDisplay');
      
      if (!walletDisplay) {
        console.error('Wallet display element not found');
        return;
      }
      
      // Handle different response formats
      let balance = 0;
      
      if (result && typeof result === 'object') {
        if (result.success && typeof result.balance === 'number') {
          balance = result.balance;
        } else if (typeof result.balance === 'number') {
          balance = result.balance;
        } else if (result.walletBalance !== undefined) {
          balance = result.walletBalance;
        }
      } else if (typeof result === 'number') {
        balance = result;
      }
      
      walletDisplay.textContent = '₹' + balance.toFixed(2);
      console.log('✅ Operator wallet display updated to:', balance);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      console.error('❌ Operator wallet fetch error:', error);
      const walletDisplay = document.getElementById('opWalletDisplay');
      if (walletDisplay) {
        walletDisplay.textContent = '₹0.00 (Error)';
      }
    })
    .getOperatorWalletBalanceDirect(currentUserId);
}

// Load operator wallet with retry mechanism
function loadOperatorWalletWithRetry() {
  let attempts = 0;
  const maxAttempts = 3;
  
  function tryLoad() {
    attempts++;
    console.log('Operator wallet load attempt', attempts);
    
    getOperatorWalletBalance();
    
    // Retry if needed
    if (attempts < maxAttempts) {
      setTimeout(tryLoad, 800);
    }
  }
  
  tryLoad();
}
// Load operator counter allocation status
function loadOperatorCounterStatus() {
  console.log('Checking counter allocation for:', currentUserId);
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      console.log('Counter status result:', result);
      
      const statusCard = document.getElementById('opCounterStatusCard');
      const statusText = document.getElementById('opCounterStatusDisplay');
      
      if (!statusCard || !statusText) {
        console.error('Counter status elements not found');
        return;
      }
      
    if (result.success && result.allocated) {
        if (result.isPrevDay) {
          // Previous day counter — show warning only in UI card
          // Button state is handled by _doOperatorLiveRefresh via mustCloseFirst
          statusCard.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, #e67e22 0%, #d35400 100%)';
          statusText.innerHTML =
            '⚠️ COUNTER ' + result.counterNo + '<br>' +
            '<small style="font-size:11px;">Kal ka counter close karo!</small>';
          // DO NOT call setOperatorButtonState here — live refresh handles it correctly

        } else {
          // Today's counter — normal
          statusCard.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, #2ecc71 0%, #27ae60 100%)';
          statusText.innerHTML =
            '✅ COUNTER ' + result.counterNo + '<br>' +
            '<small style="font-size: 12px;">Allocated</small>';
          enableOperatorForms();

          // Remove old banner if any
          var oldBanner = document.getElementById('prevDayCounterBanner');
          if (oldBanner) oldBanner.remove();
        }

        console.log('✅ Counter allocated:', result.counterNo, 'isPrevDay:', result.isPrevDay);

      } else {
        // Counter not allocated — only update card display, DO NOT disable forms
        // live refresh (mustCloseFirst) decides actual button state
        statusCard.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, #e74c3c 0%, #c0392b 100%)';
        statusText.textContent = '⛔ NOT ALLOCATED';
        // NOTE: Do NOT call disableOperatorForms() here — let live refresh handle it

        console.log('⛔ Counter not allocated');
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      console.error('Counter status error:', error);
      
      const statusCard = document.getElementById('opCounterStatusCard');
      const statusText = document.getElementById('opCounterStatusDisplay');
      
      if (statusCard && statusText) {
        statusCard.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, #e74c3c 0%, #c0392b 100%)';
        statusText.textContent = '⛔ ERROR';
      }
      
      disableOperatorForms();
    })
    .getOperatorCounterStatus(currentUserId);
}

  console.log('Getting supervisor wallet balance for:', currentUserId);
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      console.log('Supervisor wallet result:', result);
      
      const walletDisplay = document.getElementById('supWalletDisplay');
      
      if (!walletDisplay) {
        console.error('Wallet display element not found');
        return;
      }
      
      // Handle different response formats
      let balance = 0;
      
      if (result && typeof result === 'object') {
        if (result.success && typeof result.balance === 'number') {
          balance = result.balance;
        } else if (typeof result.balance === 'number') {
          balance = result.balance;
        } else if (result.walletBalance !== undefined) {
          balance = result.walletBalance;
        }
      } else if (typeof result === 'number') {
        balance = result;
      }
      
      walletDisplay.textContent = '₹' + balance.toFixed(2);

    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {

// ✅ FIX #3: Load operator day status
function loadOperatorDayStatus(branchCode) {
  dayBranchCache = branchCode; // Cache branch
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      const statusCard = document.getElementById('opDayStatusCard');
      const statusText = document.getElementById('opDayStatusDisplay');
      
      dayStartedCache = result.started; // Cache status
      
      if (result.started) {
        if (statusCard) statusCard.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, #2ecc71 0%, #27ae60 100%)';
        if (statusText) statusText.textContent = '✅ DAY OPEN';
        // ✅ FIX: Do NOT call enableOperatorForms here.
        // Form state must be driven by counter allocation (loadOperatorCounterStatus).
        // Enabling forms just because day started (without counter) is wrong.
      } else {
        if (statusCard) statusCard.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg, #e74c3c 0%, #c0392b 100%)';
        if (statusText) statusText.textContent = '⛔ DAY CLOSED';
        disableOperatorForms();
      }
    })
    .isDayStarted(branchCode);
}

// ✅ Enable/disable operator forms
// ── Operator button state manager ─────────────────────────────
// mode: 'COUNTER_OPEN'    → sab enable (normal working state)
//       'PREV_DAY_OPEN'   → sirf Close Counter + Return Cash enable, baki disable
//       'COUNTER_CLOSED'  → sirf Logout enable, sab disable
//       'NO_COUNTER'      → sirf Logout enable, sab disable
function setOperatorButtonState(mode) {
  const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.action-card');
  buttons.forEach(function(btn) {
    const txt = (btn.textContent || '').trim();

    // Logout — hamesha enabled
    if (txt.includes('Logout')) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.style.opacity = '1';
      btn.style.cursor = 'pointer';
      btn.title = '';
      return;
    }

    if (mode === 'COUNTER_OPEN') {
      // Sab enable
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.style.opacity = '1';
      btn.style.cursor = 'pointer';
      btn.title = '';

    } else if (mode === 'PREV_DAY_OPEN') {
      // Sirf Close Counter aur Return Cash enable
      if (txt.includes('Close Counter') || txt.includes('Return Cash')) {
        btn.disabled = false;
        btn.style.opacity = '1';
        btn.style.cursor = 'pointer';
        btn.title = '';
      } else {
        btn.disabled = true;
        btn.style.opacity = '0.35';
        btn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
        btn.title = '⚠️ Pichle din ka counter close karo pehle';
      }

    } else {
      // COUNTER_CLOSED / NO_COUNTER — sab disable
      btn.disabled = true;
      btn.style.opacity = '0.35';
      btn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
      btn.title = mode === 'COUNTER_CLOSED'
        ? '✅ Counter close ho gaya — logout karo'
        : '⚠️ Counter allocate nahi hai — supervisor se contact karo';
    }
  });
}

// Legacy wrappers — purane calls break na hon
function enableOperatorForms()  { setOperatorButtonState('COUNTER_OPEN');   }
function disableOperatorForms() { setOperatorButtonState('NO_COUNTER');     }

loadSupervisorWalletWithRetry();

// Initialize supervisor wallet if doesn't exist
function initializeSupervisorWallet() {

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      console.log('Wallet initialization:', result);

        loadSupervisorWallet();
      }, 500);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      console.error('Wallet init error:', error);
      loadSupervisorWallet(); // Try to load anyway
    })
    .ensureSupervisorWallet(currentUserId);
}

// Load supervisor wallet with retry mechanism
function loadSupervisorWalletWithRetry() {
  let attempts = 0;
  const maxAttempts = 3;
  
  function tryLoad() {
    attempts++;
    console.log('Wallet load attempt', attempts);
    
    getSupervisorWalletBalance();
    
    // Retry if needed
    if (attempts < maxAttempts) {
      setTimeout(tryLoad, 1000);
    }
  }
  
  tryLoad();
}
// NAYA CODE — SAHI
function loadSupervisorDayStatus(branchCode) {
  dayBranchCache = branchCode;
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      // ✅ FIX: isDayStarted() boolean return karta hai, result object nahi
      // result directly true/false hai, result.started nahi
      const isOpen = (result === true);
      dayStartedCache = isOpen;
      updateDayStatusUI(isOpen ? 'OPEN' : 'CLOSED');
      sessionStorage.setItem('dayStatus', isOpen ? 'OPEN' : 'CLOSED');
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      console.log('Day status load error:', error);
      // ✅ Error pe bhi sessionStorage se restore karo, 'CLOSED' default mat lo
      const stored = sessionStorage.getItem('dayStatus') || 'CLOSED';
      updateDayStatusUI(stored);
    })
    .isDayStarted(branchCode);
}

// ✅ FIX #4: Load operators with wallets
function loadSupervisorOperators() {
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result.success) {
        displaySupervisorOperators(result.operators || []);
      }
    })
    .getOperatorsWithWallets(currentUserId);
}

function displaySupervisorOperators(operators) {
  const container = document.getElementById('operatorsWalletList');
  
  if (operators.length === 0) {
    container.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #7f8c8d;">No operators found in your branch</p>';
    return;
  }
  
  let html = '';
  operators.forEach(function(op) {
    html += '<div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin-bottom: 10px; display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center;">';
    html += '<div>';
    html += '<h4 style="margin: 0 0 5px 0; color: #2c3e50;">' + op.userId + '</h4>';
    html += '<div style="color: #7f8c8d; font-size: 12px;">Branch: ' + op.branchCode + '</div>';
    html += '<div style="font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold; color: #f39c12; margin-top: 5px;">₹' + (op.balance || 0).toFixed(2) + '</div>';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '<button onclick="supervisorTransferCash(\'' + op.userId.replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\')" style="padding: 10px 15px; background: linear-gradient(135deg, #3498db, #2980b9); color: white; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold;">💸 Transfer</button>';
    html += '</div>';
  });
  
  container.innerHTML = html;
}

function supervisorStartDay() {
  const branchCode = sessionStorage.getItem('branchCode');
  
  if (!currentUserId || !branchCode) {
    alert('Session expired. Please login again.');
    return;
  }
  
  // ✅ REMOVED - No cash prompt, just confirm
  if (!confirm('Start day operations for today?')) {
    return;
  }
  
  // Disable button and show loading
  const btnStartDay = document.getElementById('btnStartDay');
  if (btnStartDay) {
    btnStartDay.disabled = true;
    btnStartDay.textContent = '⏳ Starting...';
  }
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result.success) {
        sessionStorage.setItem('dayStatus', 'OPEN');
        sessionStorage.removeItem('isPreviousDay');
        sessionStorage.removeItem('openDayDate');
        updateDayStatusUI('OPEN');
        // Show date on screen
        const dateEl = document.getElementById('currentDayDateDisplay');
        if (dateEl) {
          const today = new Date();
          dateEl.textContent = today.toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {day:'2-digit',month:'short',year:'numeric'});
          dateEl.style.display = 'inline';
        }
        alert('✅ Day started successfully!\n\nDate: ' + new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-IN'));
        loadSupervisorDetailsNew();
        // ✅ FIX: Operator refresh force karo — taaki forms enable ho jaayein
        window._opPrevDay     = undefined;
        window._opPrevCounter = undefined;
        if (typeof startOperatorLiveRefresh === 'function') startOperatorLiveRefresh();
      } else {
        if (result.alreadyDoneToday) {
          // ✅ FIX: Aaj ka Day Begin + Day End dono ho chuke — button lock karo
          sessionStorage.setItem('dayStatus', 'DONE_TODAY');
          updateDayStatusUI('DONE_TODAY');
          alert('🔒 Aaj ka Din Complete Ho Chuka Hai!\n\nDay Begin aur Day End dono ho chuke hain.\nKal hi dobara Day Begin kar sakte ho.');
        } else if (result.isPreviousDay) {
          // Previous day not closed — redirect to Day End
          showPreviousDayAlert(result.openDayDate);
          if (btnStartDay) { btnStartDay.disabled = false; btnStartDay.style.background='linear-gradient(135deg,#2ecc71,#27ae60)'; btnStartDay.style.opacity='1'; btnStartDay.textContent = '▶️ Start Day'; }
        } else if (result.message && result.message.toLowerCase().indexOf('already') !== -1) {
          // Day already started (OPEN) — update UI to OPEN state
          sessionStorage.setItem('dayStatus', 'OPEN');
          updateDayStatusUI('OPEN');
          const dateEl = document.getElementById('currentDayDateDisplay');
          if (dateEl) {
            const today = new Date();
            dateEl.textContent = today.toLocaleDateString('en-IN', {day:'2-digit',month:'short',year:'numeric'});
            dateEl.style.display = 'inline';
          }
        } else {
          alert('❌ ' + result.message);
          if (btnStartDay) { btnStartDay.disabled = false; btnStartDay.style.background='linear-gradient(135deg,#2ecc71,#27ae60)'; btnStartDay.style.opacity='1'; btnStartDay.textContent = '▶️ Start Day'; }
        }
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      alert('❌ Failed: ' + error.message);
      if (btnStartDay) { btnStartDay.disabled = false; btnStartDay.style.background='linear-gradient(135deg,#2ecc71,#27ae60)'; btnStartDay.style.opacity='1'; btnStartDay.textContent = '▶️ Start Day'; }
    })
    .supervisorStartDay(currentUserId, branchCode, currentUserToken);
}

function supervisorEndDay() {
  const branchCode = sessionStorage.getItem('branchCode');
  if (!currentUserId || !branchCode) {
    alert('⚠️ Session expired. Login again.');
    return;
  }

  _showDayEndCheckModal(branchCode);
}

function _showDayEndCheckModal(branchCode) {
  const old = document.getElementById('dayEndCheckModal');
  if (old) old.remove();

  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'dayEndCheckModal';
  modal.style.cssText =
    'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.65);' +
    'z-index:9999;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;overflow-y:auto;';

  modal.innerHTML =
    '<div style="background:white;border-radius:16px;padding:30px;max-width:480px;width:92%;text-align:center;">' +
      '<div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:12px;">🔍</div>' +
      '<p style="font-weight:bold;color:#2c3e50;font-size:16px;">Counter check ho rahi hai...</p>' +
    '</div>';

  document.body.appendChild(modal);

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (!result.success) {
        modal.remove();
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
        return;
      }
      _renderDayEndModal(modal, result, branchCode);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      modal.remove();
      alert('❌ Error: ' + err.message);
    })
    .getBranchCounterStatus(currentUserId);
}

function _renderDayEndModal(modal, status, branchCode) {
  const allClosed = status.allClosed;
  const counters  = status.counters || [];
  const totalOpen = status.totalOpen || 0;

  let counterRows = '';
  if (counters.length === 0) {
    counterRows =
      '<div style="background:#d4edda;border-radius:8px;padding:12px;color:#155724;font-size:14px;">' +
        '✅ Aaj koi counter allocate nahi tha.' +
      '</div>';
  } else {
    counters.forEach(function(c) {
      const isOpen      = c.isOpen;
      const rowBg       = isOpen ? '#fff3cd' : '#d4edda';
      const statusColor = isOpen ? '#856404' : '#155724';
      const statusIcon  = isOpen ? '🔴 OPEN' : '🟢 CLOSED';
      const balText     = c.walletBalance > 0
        ? '<span style="color:#e74c3c;font-weight:bold;">₹' + c.walletBalance.toFixed(2) + '</span>'
        : '<span style="color:#27ae60;">₹0.00 ✓</span>';
      const pendText    = c.pendingCount > 0
        ? '<span style="color:#e74c3c;font-weight:bold;">' + c.pendingCount + ' pending</span>'
        : '<span style="color:#27ae60;">0 ✓</span>';

      counterRows +=
        '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 90px 80px 85px;gap:8px;align-items:center;' +
          'background:' + rowBg + ';border-radius:8px;padding:10px 12px;margin-bottom:8px;">' +
          '<span style="font-weight:600;color:#2c3e50;font-size:14px;">👤 ' + c.operatorId + '</span>' +
          '<span style="font-size:12px;color:' + statusColor + ';font-weight:bold;">' + statusIcon + '</span>' +
          '<span style="font-size:12px;">' + balText + '</span>' +
          '<span style="font-size:12px;">' + pendText + '</span>' +
        '</div>';
    });
  }

  let summaryHtml;
  if (allClosed) {
    summaryHtml =
      '<div style="background:#d4edda;border-radius:10px;padding:14px;margin-bottom:20px;text-align:center;">' +
        '<p style="margin:0;color:#155724;font-weight:bold;font-size:15px;">✅ Sab counters band hain!</p>' +
        '<p style="margin:5px 0 0 0;color:#155724;font-size:13px;">Day end allowed.</p>' +
      '</div>';
  } else {
    summaryHtml =
      '<div style="background:#f8d7da;border-radius:10px;padding:14px;margin-bottom:20px;text-align:center;">' +
        '<p style="margin:0;color:#721c24;font-weight:bold;font-size:15px;">⛔ ' + totalOpen + ' counter OPEN</p>' +
        '<p style="margin:5px 0 0 0;color:#721c24;font-size:13px;">Pehle counters band karo.</p>' +
      '</div>';
  }

  const colHeader = counters.length > 0
    ? '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 90px 80px 85px;gap:8px;' +
        'padding:6px 12px;margin-bottom:6px;">' +
        '<span style="font-size:11px;color:#7f8c8d;font-weight:bold;">OPERATOR</span>' +
        '<span style="font-size:11px;color:#7f8c8d;font-weight:bold;">STATUS</span>' +
        '<span style="font-size:11px;color:#7f8c8d;font-weight:bold;">WALLET</span>' +
        '<span style="font-size:11px;color:#7f8c8d;font-weight:bold;">ENTRIES</span>' +
      '</div>'
    : '';

  const actionBtns = allClosed
    ? '<div style="display:flex;gap:10px;margin-top:20px;">' +
        '<button onclick="document.getElementById(\'dayEndCheckModal\').remove()" ' +
          'style="flex:1;padding:12px;background:#ecf0f1;border:none;border-radius:8px;' +
          'font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;color:#2c3e50;">Cancel</button>' +
        '<button onclick="_confirmEndDay()" id="confirmEndDayBtn" ' +
          'style="flex:1;padding:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#e74c3c,#c0392b);' +
          'border:none;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;color:white;">⏹️ Day End</button>' +
      '</div>'
    : '<div style="margin-top:20px;">' +
        '<button onclick="document.getElementById(\'dayEndCheckModal\').remove()" ' +
          'style="width:100%;padding:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#667eea,#764ba2);' +
          'border:none;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;color:white;">OK</button>' +
      '</div>';

  modal.innerHTML =
    '<div style="background:white;border-radius:16px;padding:28px;max-width:500px;width:94%;' +
      'max-height:90vh;overflow-y:auto;box-shadow:0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);">' +
      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:20px;">' +
        '<h3 style="margin:0;color:#2c3e50;font-size:18px;">⏹️ Day End Check</h3>' +
        '<span style="font-size:12px;color:#7f8c8d;">Branch: ' + branchCode + '</span>' +
      '</div>' +
      summaryHtml +
      '<h4 style="color:#2c3e50;margin:0 0 10px 0;font-size:14px;">🖥️ Counter Status</h4>' +
      colHeader +
      counterRows +
      actionBtns +
    '</div>';
}

function _confirmEndDay() {
  const btn = document.getElementById('confirmEndDayBtn');
  if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = '⏳ Processing...'; }

  const branchCode = sessionStorage.getItem('branchCode');

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      const modal = document.getElementById('dayEndCheckModal');
      if (modal) modal.remove();

     if (result.success) {
    sessionStorage.setItem('dayStatus', 'DONE_TODAY');
    sessionStorage.removeItem('isPreviousDay');
    sessionStorage.removeItem('openDayDate');
    if (typeof updateDayStatusUI === 'function') updateDayStatusUI('DONE_TODAY');
    if (typeof loadSupervisorDetailsNew === 'function') loadSupervisorDetailsNew();
    stopSupervisorLiveRefresh();
    window._opPrevDay     = undefined;
    window._opPrevCounter = undefined;
    if (typeof startOperatorLiveRefresh === 'function') startOperatorLiveRefresh();

    _showSuccessModal('Day End! ✅', result.message + '\n\nAaj ka din complete. Kal dobara Begin karo.', '#8e44ad');
        const dateEl = document.getElementById('currentDayDateDisplay');
        if (dateEl) dateEl.style.display = 'none';
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
        if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '⏹️ Day End'; }
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      const modal = document.getElementById('dayEndCheckModal');
      if (modal) modal.remove();
      alert('❌ Error: ' + err.message);
    })
    .endDay(currentUserId, branchCode, currentUserToken);
}
// ✅ FIX #5: SUPERVISOR TRANSFER CASH
function supervisorTransferCash(operatorId) {
  if (!dayStartedCache) {
    alert('⚠️ Day Not Started!\n\nPlease start the day before transferring cash.');
    return;
  }
  
  const amount = prompt('Transfer amount to ' + operatorId + ' (₹):');
  
  if (!amount || isNaN(amount) || parseFloat(amount) <= 0) {
    return;
  }
  
  const btn = event.target;
  const originalText = btn.textContent;
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = 'Processing...';
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = originalText;
      
      if (result.success) {
        alert('✅ Transfer successful!\n\nAmount: ₹' + amount + '\nTo: ' + operatorId);
        loadSupervisorDetailsNew();
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = originalText;
      alert('❌ Error: ' + error.message);
    })
    .transferCashToOperator(currentUserId, operatorId, parseFloat(amount), 'Cash allocation', currentUserToken);
}

// ✅ FIX #5: OPERATOR RETURN CASH
function operatorReturnCash() {
  const walletText = document.getElementById('opWalletDisplay').textContent;
  const balance = parseFloat(walletText.replace('₹', '').replace(',', ''));
  
  if (balance <= 0) {
    alert('No cash to return! Wallet balance: ₹0');
    return;
  }
  
  if (!dayStartedCache) {
    alert('⚠️ Day Not Started!\n\nCannot return cash when day is closed.');
    return;
  }
  
  const amount = prompt('Return amount to supervisor (Available: ₹' + balance.toFixed(2) + '):');
  
  if (!amount || isNaN(amount) || parseFloat(amount) <= 0) {
    return;
  }
  
  if (parseFloat(amount) > balance) {
    alert('❌ Insufficient balance!');
    return;
  }
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result.success) {
        alert('✅ Cash returned successfully!\n\nAmount: ₹' + amount);
        loadOperatorWallet();
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
      }
    })
    .returnCashToSupervisor(currentUserId, parseFloat(amount), 'Day close return');
}


// ✅ FIX #6: CASH RECEIPT BANNER
function showCashReceiptBanner(amount) {
  const existingBanner = document.getElementById('cashReceiptBanner');
  if (existingBanner) existingBanner.remove();
  
  const banner = document.createElement('div');
  banner.id = 'cashReceiptBanner';
  banner.style.cssText = 'position: fixed; top: 80px; left: 50%; transform: translateX(-50%); background: linear-gradient(135deg, #2ecc71, #27ae60); color: white; padding: 25px 40px; border-radius: 15px; z-index: 9999; box-shadow: 0 8px 32px rgba(0,0,0,0.3); animation: bounceIn 0.5s; text-align: center; min-width: 300px;';
  
  banner.innerHTML = `
    <h3 style="margin: 0 0 10px 0; font-size: 22px; font-weight: bold;">💰 Cash Received!</h3>
    <p style="margin: 0 0 15px 0; font-size: 32px; font-weight: bold;">₹${amount.toFixed(2)}</p>
    <button onclick="this.parentElement.remove()" style="padding: 10px 25px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.3); border: 2px solid white; color: white; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold; font-size: 14px;">
      ✓ Got it!
    </button>
  `;
  
  document.body.appendChild(banner);
  
  setTimeout(() => {
    if (banner.parentElement) banner.remove();
  }, 10000);
}

// ============================================
// OPERATOR FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function loadOperatorData() {
  console.log('Loading operator dashboard');
  loadOperatorRejectedEntries();
}

function openOperatorForm(formType) {
  // ✅ Check counter allocation before opening form
  if (!currentUserId) {
    alert('❌ Error: User not logged in');
    return;
  }
  
  // Check if counter is allocated
  showLoadingOverlay('Checking counter status...');
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(counterResult) {
      hideLoadingOverlay();
      
      if (!counterResult.success || !counterResult.allocated) {
        alert('⚠️ Counter Not Allocated!\n\n' + 
              'You must have an allocated counter before making transactions.\n\n' +
              'Please contact your supervisor to allocate a counter.');
        return;
      }
      
      // Counter allocated, proceed to open form
      proceedToOpenForm(formType, counterResult.counterNo);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoadingOverlay();
      alert('❌ Error checking counter status: ' + error.message);
    })
    .getOperatorCounterStatus(currentUserId);
}

/**
 * Proceed to open operator form after counter check
 */
function proceedToOpenForm(formType, counterNo) {
  const formNames = {
    'member-entry': 'Member Entry',
    'account-open': 'Account Open',
    'deposit': 'Deposit Entry',
    'loan': 'Loan Entry',
    'loan-repayment': 'Loan Repayment',
    'account-close': 'Account Close',
    'passbook-print': 'PassbookPrint',
     'savings':'Savings Account',   
  'modify': 'Modify Member/Account'  
  };
  
  alert('⚠️ OPERATOR MODE\n\n' +
        'Counter: ' + counterNo + '\n' +
        'Opening: ' + formNames[formType] + '\n\n' +
        '📝 Note: All entries you submit will go to PENDING status.\n' +
        '✅ Supervisor must approve before saving to final sheets.\n\n' +
        'Form will open in new window...');
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(url) {
      if (url) {
        const formUrl = url + '?page=' + formType 
              + '&operatorId=' + currentUserId 
              + '&operator='   + currentUserId 
              + '&branch='     + dayBranchCache
              + '&token='      + encodeURIComponent(currentUserToken);  // ✅ TOKEN ADD
        window.open(formUrl, '_blank');
      } else {
        alert('Error: Could not get form URL');
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      alert('Error opening form: ' + error.message);
    })
    .getWebAppUrl();
}
function showOperatorRejected() {
  document.getElementById('rejectedEntriesSection').classList.remove('hidden');
  loadOperatorRejectedEntries();
  
  document.getElementById('rejectedEntriesSection').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
}

function loadOperatorRejectedEntries() {
  const listDiv = document.getElementById('rejectedEntriesList');
  if (!listDiv) return;
  
  listDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading"><div class="spinner"></div>Loading rejected entries...</div>';
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.success) {
        displayRejectedEntries(res.entries || []);
        document.getElementById('rejectedCountBadge').textContent = res.entries.length;
      } else {
        listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:white;text-align:center;">Error loading entries</p>';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:white;text-align:center;">Error: ' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</p>';
    })
    .getOperatorRejectedEntries(currentUserId);
}

function displayRejectedEntries(entries) {
  const listDiv = document.getElementById('rejectedEntriesList');
  
  if (entries.length === 0) {
    listDiv.innerHTML = `
      <div style="text-align: center; padding: 40px; background: rgba(40,167,69,0.2); border-radius: 12px;">
        <div style="font-size: 64px; margin-bottom: 15px;">✅</div>
        <h3 style="color: #28a745; margin: 0 0 10px 0;">No Rejected Entries</h3>
        <p style="color: white; margin: 0;">All your entries are either approved or pending approval!</p>
      </div>
    `;
    return;
  }
  
  let html = '';
  
  entries.forEach(entry => {
    let data = {};
    try {
      data = JSON.parse(entry.dataJSON);
    } catch (e) {
      data = {};
    }
    
    const previewFields = Object.keys(data).slice(0, 3).map(key => `<strong>${escapeHtml(key)}:</strong> ${escapeHtml(String(data[key] || ''))}`).join('<br>'); // ✅ XSS fix
    
    html += `
      <div class="approval-card" style="border-left-color: #dc3545;">
        <div style="margin-bottom: 10px;">
          <strong style="color: #FFD700; font-size: 16px;">${escapeHtml(entry.type)}</strong>
          <span style="float: right; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.7); font-size: 12px;">${escapeHtml(entry.submitted)}</span>
        </div>
        <div style="color: white; font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 8px;">
          Entry ID: <strong>${escapeHtml(entry.entryId)}</strong>
        </div>
        <div style="background: rgba(255,255,255,0.05); padding: 10px; border-radius: 6px; margin-bottom: 10px; font-size: 12px; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.8);">
          ${previewFields}
        </div>
        <div style="background: rgba(220,53,69,0.2); padding: 10px; border-radius: 6px; margin-bottom: 10px; border-left: 3px solid #dc3545;">
          <strong style="color: #dc3545;">❌ Rejection Reason:</strong><br>
          <span style="color: white; font-size: 13px; margin-top: 5px; display: block;">${escapeHtml(entry.notes)}</span> <!-- ✅ XSS fix -->
        </div>
        <div class="approval-actions">
          <button onclick="modifyRejectedEntry(${entry.rowIndex}, '${entry.entryId}')" style="background: #007bff; color: white; padding: 10px 15px; border: none; border-radius: 6px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold;">
            ✏️ Modify & Resubmit
          </button>
          <button onclick="deleteRejectedEntry(${entry.rowIndex}, '${entry.entryId}')" class="btn-danger" style="padding: 10px 15px; border-radius: 6px; font-weight: bold;">
            🗑️ Delete Permanently
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  });
  
  listDiv.innerHTML = html;
}

function modifyRejectedEntry(rowIndex, entryId) {
  alert('🔄 MODIFY ENTRY\n\n' +
        'Entry ID: ' + entryId + '\n\n' +
        '📝 Feature: Modify rejected entry data and resubmit for approval.\n\n' +
        'This feature requires form integration.\n' +
        'Contact admin to enable this functionality.');
}

function deleteRejectedEntry(rowIndex, entryId) {
  if (!confirm('⚠️ DELETE REJECTED ENTRY\n\n' +
               'Entry ID: ' + entryId + '\n\n' +
               'This will permanently delete this rejected entry.\n\n' +
               'Are you sure?')) {
    return;
  }
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.success) {
        alert('✅ Entry deleted successfully!');
        loadOperatorRejectedEntries();
      } else {
        alert('❌ Error: ' + res.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      alert('❌ Error: ' + err.message);
    })
    .deleteRejectedEntry(rowIndex, currentUserId);
}

function operatorLogout() {
  if (confirm('Are you sure you want to logout?')) {
    stopWalletAutoRefresh(); // ✅ FIX #7: Stop auto-refresh
    location.reload();
  }
}

// Load pending entries count for badge
function loadPendingCount() {
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result.success) {
        const badge = document.getElementById('pendingCountBadge');
        if (badge) {
          badge.textContent = result.count || 0;
        }
      }
    })
    .getPendingEntries(currentUserId);
}


function loadPendingApprovals() {
  const listDiv = document.getElementById('pendingApprovalsList');
  if (!listDiv) {
    console.error('❌ pendingApprovalsList element not found!');
    return;
  }
  
  if (!currentUserId) {
    console.error('❌ currentUserId is not set!');
    listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:white;text-align:center;">⚠️ Session expired. Please login again.</p>';
    return;
  }
  
  console.log('🔄 Loading pending approvals for:', currentUserId);
  listDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading"><div class="spinner"></div>Loading pending approvals...</div>';
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      console.log('✅ RAW RESPONSE:', res);
      console.log('Response type:', typeof res);
      console.log('res.success:', res.success);
      console.log('res.entries:', res.entries);
      console.log('res.count:', res.count);
      console.log('res.message:', res.message);
      
      // ✅ CRITICAL FIX: Check if response is valid
      if (!res) {
        console.error('❌ Response is null or undefined');
        listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#ff6b6b;text-align:center;">❌ No response from server</p>';
        return;
      }
      
      // ✅ Check success flag
      if (res.success === true) {
        console.log('✅ Success flag is TRUE');
        
        // ✅ Validate entries array
        if (!res.entries) {
          console.warn('⚠️ res.entries is undefined');
          res.entries = [];
        }
        
        if (!Array.isArray(res.entries)) {
          console.error('❌ res.entries is not an array:', typeof res.entries);
          listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#ff6b6b;text-align:center;">❌ Invalid data format</p>';
          return;
        }
        
        console.log('📊 Total entries to display:', res.entries.length);
        
        try {
          // Call display function
          displayPendingApprovals(res.entries);
          
          // Update badge
          const badge = document.getElementById('pendingCountBadge');
          if (badge) {
            badge.textContent = res.count || res.entries.length || 0;
            console.log('✅ Badge updated to:', badge.textContent);
          }
          
          console.log('✅ Display completed successfully');
          
        } catch (displayError) {
          console.error('❌ Display function error:', displayError);
          console.error('Error stack:', displayError.stack);
          listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#ff6b6b;text-align:center;">❌ Display Error: ' + escapeHtml(displayError.message) + '</p>';
        }
        
      } else {
        // Success is false
        console.error('❌ Success flag is FALSE');
        console.error('Error message:', res.message);
        listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#ff6b6b;text-align:center;">❌ ' + escapeHtml(res.message || 'Error loading approvals') + '</p>';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      console.error('❌ API FAILURE:', err);
      console.error('Error message:', err.message);
      listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#ff6b6b;text-align:center;">❌ Server Error: ' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</p>';
    })
    .getPendingEntries(currentUserId);
}


function displayPendingApprovals(entries) {
  console.log('🎨 displayPendingApprovals called with:', entries);
  
  const listDiv = document.getElementById('pendingApprovalsList');
  
  if (!listDiv) {
    console.error('❌ pendingApprovalsList div not found in DOM');
    return;
  }
  
  // ✅ Validate input
  if (!entries) {
    console.error('❌ entries parameter is null/undefined');
    entries = [];
  }
  
  if (!Array.isArray(entries)) {
    console.error('❌ entries is not an array:', typeof entries);
    listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#ff6b6b;text-align:center;">❌ Invalid entries data type</p>';
    return;
  }
  
  console.log('📊 Displaying', entries.length, 'entries');
  
  // If no entries
  if (entries.length === 0) {
    console.log('✅ No entries - showing success message');
    listDiv.innerHTML = `
      <div style="text-align: center; padding: 40px; background: rgba(40,167,69,0.2); border-radius: 12px;">
        <div style="font-size: 64px; margin-bottom: 15px;">✅</div>
        <h3 style="color: #28a745; margin: 0 0 10px 0;">All Caught Up!</h3>
        <p style="color: white; margin: 0;">No pending approvals at this time.</p>
      </div>
    `;
    return;
  }
  
  // Build HTML
  let html = '';
  
  for (let i = 0; i < entries.length; i++) {
    const entry = entries[i];
    console.log('🔍 Processing entry', i + 1, ':', entry);
    
    try {
      // ✅ Validate entry object
      if (!entry) {
        console.warn('⚠️ Entry', i, 'is null/undefined - skipping');
        continue;
      }
      
      // ✅ Extract safe values with defaults
      const entryId = String(entry.entryId || 'N/A');
      const type = String(entry.type || 'UNKNOWN').trim().toUpperCase();
      const operator = String(entry.operator || 'N/A');
      const submitted = String(entry.submitted || 'N/A');
      const rowIndex = parseInt(entry.rowIndex) || 0;
      
      console.log('  - Type:', type);
      console.log('  - Operator:', operator);
      console.log('  - Entry ID:', entryId);
      
      // ✅ Parse JSON data
      let data = {};
      try {
        if (entry.dataJSON && entry.dataJSON.trim() !== '') {
          data = JSON.parse(entry.dataJSON);
          console.log('  - Data parsed successfully:', Object.keys(data));
        } else {
          console.warn('  - dataJSON is empty');
        }
      } catch (parseError) {
        console.error('  - JSON Parse Error:', parseError.message);
        console.error('  - Raw JSON:', entry.dataJSON);
        data = { _error: 'Invalid JSON' };
      }
      
      // ✅ Generate preview - SIMPLIFIED VERSION
      let previewHTML = '<div style="color: rgba(255,255,255,0.7); font-size: 13px;">';
      
      // Show first 5 fields from data
      const keys = Object.keys(data).slice(0, 15);
      if (keys.length > 0) {
        keys.forEach(key => {
          const value = data[key] || 'N/A';
          previewHTML += `<div style="margin-bottom: 5px;"><strong style="color: #4facfe;">${escapeHtml(key)}:</strong> ${escapeHtml(String(value))}</div>`; // ✅ XSS fix
        });
      } else {
        previewHTML += '<div>No data available</div>';
      }
      
      previewHTML += '</div>';
      
      // ✅ Build card HTML - SIMPLE VERSION
      html += `
        <div style="margin-bottom: 15px; padding: 15px; background: rgba(255,255,255,0.05); border-radius: 10px; border: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.2);">
          <div style="margin-bottom: 10px; color: white;">
            <strong style="color: #FFD700; font-size: 16px;">${escapeHtml(type)}</strong>
            <span style="float: right; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.6); font-size: 12px;">${escapeHtml(submitted)}</span>
          </div>
          <div style="color: rgba(255,255,255,0.8); font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 10px;">
            <strong>Submitted by:</strong> ${escapeHtml(operator)}<br>
            <strong>Entry ID:</strong> ${escapeHtml(entryId)}
          </div>
          <div style="background: rgba(0,0,0,0.2); padding: 10px; border-radius: 6px; margin-bottom: 12px;">
            <strong style="color: #FFD700; display: block; margin-bottom: 8px;">📋 Preview:</strong>
            ${previewHTML}
          </div>
          <div style="display: flex; gap: 10px;">
            <button onclick="approveEntryAction(${rowIndex}, '${entryId}', '${operator}')" 
                    style="flex: 1; padding: 12px; background: #28a745; color: white; border: none; border-radius: 6px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold;">
              ✅ Approve
            </button>
            <button onclick="rejectEntryAction(${rowIndex}, '${entryId}', '${operator}')" 
                    style="flex: 1; padding: 12px; background: #dc3545; color: white; border: none; border-radius: 6px; cursor: pointer; font-weight: bold;">
              ❌ Reject
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
      
      console.log('✅ Card HTML generated for entry', i + 1);
      
    } catch (cardError) {
      console.error('❌ Error building card for entry', i, ':', cardError);
      console.error('Error stack:', cardError.stack);
      
      // Add error card
      html += `
        <div style="margin-bottom: 15px; padding: 15px; background: rgba(220,53,69,0.1); border-radius: 10px; border: 1px solid #dc3545;">
          <div style="color: #ff6b6b;">
            <strong>⚠️ Error displaying entry ${i + 1}</strong><br>
            <small>${escapeHtml(cardError.message)}</small>
          </div>
        </div>
      `;
    }
  }
  
  // ✅ Set final HTML
  console.log('📝 Setting innerHTML with', html.length, 'characters');
  
  try {
    listDiv.innerHTML = html;
    console.log('✅ innerHTML set successfully');
  } catch (htmlError) {
    console.error('❌ Error setting innerHTML:', htmlError);
    listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#ff6b6b;">Error rendering HTML</p>';
  }
}
function testPendingApprovalsManual() {
  console.log('🧪 Testing pending approvals manually...');
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      console.log('=== MANUAL TEST RESULT ===');
      console.log('Full response object:', res);
      console.log('Type:', typeof res);
      console.log('Keys:', Object.keys(res));
      console.log('Success?', res.success);
      console.log('Message:', res.message);
      console.log('Entries:', res.entries);
      console.log('Count:', res.count);
      console.log('Branch:', res.supervisorBranch);
      console.log('========================');
      
      // Try to display
      if (res.success && res.entries) {
        displayPendingApprovals(res.entries);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      console.error('Manual test failed:', err);
    })
    .getPendingEntries(currentUserId);
}


// ============================================
// FUNCTION 4: Approve Entry Action
// ============================================
function approveEntryAction(rowIndex, entryId, operatorId) {
  const notes = prompt('✅ APPROVE ENTRY\n\n' +
                       'Entry ID: ' + entryId + '\n' +
                       'Operator: ' + operatorId + '\n\n' +
                       'Optional approval notes (or press OK to approve):');

  if (notes === null) return; // User cancelled

  const finalNotes = notes.trim() || 'Approved';

  const listDiv = document.getElementById('pendingApprovalsList');
  listDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading"><div class="spinner"></div>Approving entry...</div>';

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.success) {
        let approveMsg = '✅ Entry Approved!\n\n' +
              'Entry ID: ' + entryId + '\n' +
              'Status: Saved to final sheet\n' +
              'Operator: ' + operatorId;
        // ✅ Show wallet deduction info for Account Close
        if (res.walletDeducted) {
          approveMsg += '\n\n💳 Operator wallet deducted (settlement paid out)';
        } else if (res.walletWarning) {
          approveMsg += '\n\n⚠️ ' + res.walletWarning;
        }
        alert(approveMsg);
        loadPendingApprovals();
        // Refresh wallet display
        getSupervisorWalletBalance();
      } else {
        alert('❌ Approval Failed\n\n' + res.message);
        loadPendingApprovals();
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      alert('❌ Error: ' + err.message);
      loadPendingApprovals();
    })
    .approveEntry(entryId, currentUserId, notes.trim(), currentUserToken);
}

// ============================================
// FUNCTION 5: Reject Entry Action
// ============================================
function rejectEntryAction(rowIndex, entryId, operatorId) {
  const reason = prompt('❌ REJECT ENTRY\n\n' +
                        'Entry ID: ' + entryId + '\n' +
                        'Operator: ' + operatorId + '\n\n' +
                        '⚠️ Please provide rejection reason (required):');

  if (!reason || reason.trim() === '') {
    alert('⚠️ Rejection reason is required!');
    return;
  }

  const listDiv = document.getElementById('pendingApprovalsList');
  listDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="loading"><div class="spinner"></div>Rejecting entry...</div>';

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.success) {
        alert('❌ Entry Rejected\n\n' +
              'Entry ID: ' + entryId + '\n' +
              'Reason: ' + reason + '\n' +
              'Operator: ' + operatorId);
        loadPendingApprovals();
      } else {
        alert('❌ Rejection Failed\n\n' + res.message);
        loadPendingApprovals();
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      alert('❌ Error: ' + err.message);
      loadPendingApprovals();
    })
    // ✅ FIXED: entryId pass karo + duplicate function remove kiya
    .rejectEntry(entryId, currentUserId, reason.trim(), currentUserToken);
}


// ✅ FEATURE 1: Show Previous Day Alert Modal
function closePrevDayAlert() {
  var m = document.getElementById('prevDayAlertModal');
  if (m) m.remove();
}

    'z-index:99999;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;';

  var dateText = openDayDate || 'Unknown';

  // ✅ FIX: No nested quotes — use separate div creation
  var box = document.createElement('div');
  box.style.cssText = 'background:white;border-radius:16px;padding:30px;max-width:420px;width:92%;text-align:center;box-shadow:0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.4);';

  box.innerHTML =
    '<div style="font-size:52px;margin-bottom:12px;">⚠️</div>' +
    '<h3 style="color:#e74c3c;margin:0 0 10px 0;font-size:20px;">Previous Day Still Open!</h3>' +

    '</div>' +
    '<p style="color:#555;font-size:14px;margin-bottom:20px;">Naya Day Begin karne se pehle pichle din ka <strong>Day End</strong> karna zaroori hai.</p>' +
    '<div style="display:flex;gap:12px;">' +
      '<button onclick="closePrevDayAlert()" style="flex:1;padding:12px;background:#ecf0f1;border:none;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;color:#2c3e50;">Dismiss</button>' +
      '<button onclick="closePrevDayAlert();supervisorEndDay();" style="flex:1;padding:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#e74c3c,#c0392b);border:none;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;color:white;">⏹️ Do Day End Now</button>' +
    '</div>';

  modal.appendChild(box);
  document.body.appendChild(modal);
}

// ── FIX: Supervisor previous day mode — restricted menu ───────
// Only allows: Cash Return, Reports, Daily Account Report, Day End, Logout
function setSupervisorPreviousDayMode(openDayDate) {
  // Show banner if not already shown
  var existBanner = document.getElementById('supPrevDayBanner');
  if (!existBanner) {
    var banner = document.createElement('div');
    banner.id = 'supPrevDayBanner';
    banner.style.cssText =
      'background:linear-gradient(135deg,#c0392b,#e74c3c);color:white;' +
      'padding:14px 20px;text-align:center;font-weight:bold;font-size:14px;' +
      'border-radius:10px;margin:10px 0;';
    banner.innerHTML =
      '⚠️ Pichle din ka Day End nahi hua! (' + (openDayDate || '') + ')<br>' +
      '<span style="font-size:12px;font-weight:normal;">' +
      'Sirf Cash Return, Reports, Daily Account Report, Day End aur Logout available hai. ' +
      'Pehle Day End karo.</span>';
    var dash = document.getElementById('supervisorDashboard') ||
               document.querySelector('.supervisor-main') ||
               document.body;
    if (dash) dash.insertBefore(banner, dash.firstChild);
  }

  // Disable all action-card buttons except allowed ones
  var allowed = ['Cash Return', 'Reports', 'Daily Report', 'Daily Account', 'Day End', 'Logout'];
  document.querySelectorAll('.action-card').forEach(function(btn) {
    var txt = (btn.textContent || '').trim();
    var isAllowed = allowed.some(function(k) { return txt.includes(k); });
    if (isAllowed) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.style.opacity = '1';
      btn.style.cursor = 'pointer';
      btn.title = '';
    } else {
      btn.disabled = true;
      btn.style.opacity = '0.35';
      btn.style.cursor = 'not-allowed';
      btn.title = '⚠️ Pichle din ka Day End karo pehle (' + (openDayDate || '') + ')';
    }
  });

  // Also disable sidebar menu items except allowed
  document.querySelectorAll('.menu-item').forEach(function(item) {
    var txt = (item.textContent || '').trim();
    var isAllowed = allowed.some(function(k) { return txt.includes(k); });
    if (!isAllowed && !txt.includes('Logout')) {
      item.style.opacity = '0.4';
      item.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
      item.title = '⚠️ Pichle din ka Day End karo pehle';
    }
  });
}

function supervisorLogout() {
  if (confirm('Are you sure you want to logout?')) {
    location.reload();
  }
}

// ============================================
// LOGOUT (ENHANCED)
// ============================================
function logout() {
  if (confirm('Are you sure you want to logout?')) {
    stopWalletAutoRefresh(); // ✅ FIX #7: Stop auto-refresh
    
    currentUserId = '';
    // ✅ FIX M-1: currentUserPassword removed
    currentUserData = {};
    currentUserToken = '';
    currentUserRole = '';
    dayStartedCache = false;
    dayBranchCache = '';
    
    location.reload();
  }
}

// ============================================
// DISPLAY PHOTO FUNCTION
// ============================================
window.displayPhoto = function(photoUrl, name) {
  const firstLetter = (name || 'U').charAt(0).toUpperCase();
  
  function createImageHTML(url, letter, avatarClass) {
    if (url && url.trim() !== '') {
      return `<img src="${url}" 
                   alt="Photo" 
                   style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;"
                   onerror="this.style.display='none'; this.parentElement.innerHTML='<div class=\\'${avatarClass}\\'>${letter}</div>';">`;
    } else {
      return `<div class="${avatarClass}">${letter}</div>`;
    }
  }
  
  const sidebarPhoto = document.getElementById('sidebarPhoto');
  if (sidebarPhoto) {
    sidebarPhoto.innerHTML = createImageHTML(photoUrl, firstLetter, 'sidebar-avatar');
  }
  
  const headerAvatar = document.getElementById('headerAvatar');
  if (headerAvatar) {
    if (photoUrl && photoUrl.trim() !== '') {
      headerAvatar.innerHTML = `<img src="${photoUrl}" 
                                     alt="Photo"
                                     style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;"
                                     onerror="this.parentElement.innerHTML='<div id=\\'headerAvatarLetter\\'>${firstLetter}</div>';">`;
    } else {
      headerAvatar.innerHTML = `<div id="headerAvatarLetter">${firstLetter}</div>`;
    }
  }
  
  const profilePhotoLarge = document.querySelector('.profile-photo-large');
  if (profilePhotoLarge) {
    profilePhotoLarge.innerHTML = createImageHTML(photoUrl, firstLetter, 'profile-avatar-large');
  }
};

// ============================================
// MEMBER DASHBOARD FUNCTIONS (KEEP ALL EXISTING)
// ============================================
function switchTab(tabName) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
  
  if (event && event.target) {
    event.target.classList.add('active');
  }
  
  if (tabName === 'profile') {
    document.getElementById('profileTab').classList.add('active');
  } else if (tabName === 'contribution') {
    document.getElementById('contributionTab').classList.add('active');
  } else if (tabName === 'loans') {
    document.getElementById('loansTab').classList.add('active');
  } else if (tabName === 'calculators') {
    document.getElementById('calculatorsTab').classList.add('active');
  }
  
  closeSidebar();
}

function loadUserData(userId) {
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.success) {
        currentUserData = res.data;
        renderData(res);
      } else {
        document.getElementById("profileTab").innerHTML = "<h3>Error</h3><p>" + escapeHtml(res.message) + "</p>";
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      document.getElementById("profileTab").innerHTML = "<h3>Error</h3><p>" + escapeHtml(err.message) + "</p>";
    })
    .getUserData(userId);
}

function renderData(res) {
  const d = res.data;
  const p = d.account;
  
  if (p) {
    const memberName = p.name || 'Member';
    const memberId = p.memberId || currentUserId;
    const photoUrl = p.photoUrl || '';
    
    displayPhoto(photoUrl, memberName);
    
    document.getElementById('sidebarName').textContent = memberName;
    document.getElementById('sidebarId').textContent = 'ID: ' + memberId;
    
    document.getElementById('memberNameDisplay').textContent = memberName;
    document.getElementById('memberIdDisplay').textContent = 'Member ID: ' + memberId;
    
    let html = "<h3>Profile Information</h3>";
    html += '<div style="overflow-x:auto;"><table>';
    html += '<tr><th>Member ID</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.memberId || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>'; // ✅ XSS fix
    html += '<tr><th>Name</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.name || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>';
    html += '<tr><th>Account No</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.accountNo || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>';
    html += '<tr><th>Open Date</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.openDate || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>';
    html += '<tr><th>Account Type</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.accountType || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>';
    html += '<tr><th>Nominee</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.nominee || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>';
    html += '<tr><th>Relation</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.relation || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>';
    html += '<tr><th>Status</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.status || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>';
    html += '<tr><th>Email</th><td>' + escapeHtml(p.email || 'N/A') + '</td></tr>';
    html += '</table></div>';
    document.getElementById("profileTab").innerHTML = html;
  }
  
  let dep = d.deposits || [];
  let depHTML = "<h3>My Contribution Details</h3>";
  if (dep.length > 0) {
    depHTML += '<div style="overflow-x:auto;"><table>';
    depHTML += '<tr><th>Account</th><th>Name</th><th>Amount</th><th>Interest</th><th>Balance</th><th>Date</th><th>Month</th></tr>';
    for (var i = 0; i < dep.length; i++) {
      depHTML += '<tr>';
      depHTML += '<td>' + escapeHtml(dep[i].accountNo || '') + '</td>';
      depHTML += '<td>' + escapeHtml(dep[i].name || '') + '</td>';
      depHTML += '<td>' + (dep[i].amount || 0) + '</td>';
      depHTML += '<td>' + (dep[i].interest || 0) + '</td>';
      depHTML += '<td>' + (dep[i].currentBalance || 0) + '</td>';
      depHTML += '<td>' + escapeHtml(dep[i].date || '') + '</td>';
      depHTML += '<td>' + escapeHtml(dep[i].monthFor || '') + '</td>';
      depHTML += '</tr>';
    }
    depHTML += '</table></div>';
  } else {
    depHTML += "<p>No contribution records found.</p>";
  }
  document.getElementById("contributionTab").innerHTML = depHTML;
  
  let loans = d.loans || [];
  let loanHTML = "<h3>My Loan Details</h3>";
  if (loans.length > 0) {
    loanHTML += '<div style="overflow-x:auto;"><table>';
    loanHTML += '<tr><th>Account</th><th>Name</th><th>Type</th><th>Amount</th><th>EMI</th><th>Paid</th><th>Remaining</th><th>Status</th></tr>';
    for (var i = 0; i < loans.length; i++) {
      loanHTML += '<tr>';
      loanHTML += '<td>' + (loans[i].loanAccount || '') + '</td>';
      loanHTML += '<td>' + escapeHtml(loans[i].name || '') + '</td>';
      loanHTML += '<td>' + escapeHtml(loans[i].loanType || '') + '</td>';
      loanHTML += '<td>' + (loans[i].loanAmount || 0) + '</td>';
      loanHTML += '<td>' + (loans[i].monthlyEmi || 0) + '</td>';
      loanHTML += '<td>' + (loans[i].totalPaid || 0) + '</td>';
      loanHTML += '<td>' + (loans[i].remaining || 0) + '</td>';
      loanHTML += '<td>' + escapeHtml(loans[i].loanStatus || '') + '</td>';
      loanHTML += '</tr>';
    }
    loanHTML += '</table></div>';
  } else {
    loanHTML += "<p>No loan records found.</p>";
  }
  document.getElementById("loansTab").innerHTML = loanHTML;
}

// ============================================
// ANNOUNCEMENTS
// ============================================
function loadAnnouncements() {
  const section = document.getElementById("announcementSection");
  if (!section) return;

  section.innerHTML = '<div class="loading"><div class="spinner"></div>Loading...</div>';

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function (res) {
      if (!res.success || !res.announcements || res.announcements.length === 0) {
        section.innerHTML = "";
        return;
      }

      const ann = res.announcements[0];
      section.innerHTML = `
        <div class="announcement-banner">
          <h4>${escapeHtml(ann.title || "Announcement")}</h4>
          <p>${escapeHtml(ann.message || "")}</p>
        </div>
      ` // ✅ XSS fix;
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function (err) {
      console.error("Load member announcements error", err);
      section.innerHTML = "";
    })
    .getAnnouncements();
}

function loadStaffAnnouncements(role, containerId) {
  const section = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!section) return;

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (!res.success || !res.announcements || res.announcements.length === 0) {
        section.innerHTML = '';
        return;
      }
      const html = res.announcements.map(ann => `
        <div class="announcement-banner" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
          <h4>📢 ${ann.title || 'Announcement'}</h4>
          <p>${ann.message || ''}</p>
          <small style="opacity:0.7;">${ann.date || ''}</small>
        </div>
      `).join('');
      section.innerHTML = html;
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      console.error('Staff announcements error', err);
      section.innerHTML = '';
    })
    .getAnnouncementsForStaff(role);
}
