// PASSWORD RESET FUNCTIONS (KEEP ALL EXISTING)
// ============================================
function openReset() {
  document.getElementById("resetModal").style.display = "flex";
  document.getElementById("otpStep1").classList.remove("hidden");
  document.getElementById("otpStep2").classList.add("hidden");
  document.getElementById("resetUserId").value = "";
  document.getElementById("otpCode").value = "";
  document.getElementById("resetNew1").value = "";
  document.getElementById("resetNew2").value = "";
  hideError("resetMsg1");
  hideError("resetMsg2");
}

function closeReset() {
  document.getElementById("resetModal").style.display = "none";
}

function sendOTP() {
  const uid = document.getElementById("resetUserId").value.trim();
  const btn = document.getElementById("sendOtpBtn");
  
  hideError("resetMsg1");
  if (!uid) {
    showError("resetMsg1", "Enter User ID");
    return;
  }
  
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = "Sending...";
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = "Send OTP to Email";
      if (res.success) {
        document.getElementById("otpStep1").classList.add("hidden");
        document.getElementById("otpStep2").classList.remove("hidden");
        
        alert(res.message);
      } else {
        showError("resetMsg1", res.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = "Send OTP to Email";
      showError("resetMsg1", "Error: " + err.message);
    })
    .sendOTP(uid);
}

function verifyOTPAndReset() {
  const uid = document.getElementById("resetUserId").value.trim();
  const otp = document.getElementById("otpCode").value.trim();
  const p1 = document.getElementById("resetNew1").value;
  const p2 = document.getElementById("resetNew2").value;
  const btn = document.getElementById("verifyOtpBtn");
  
  hideError("resetMsg2");
  
  if (!otp || !p1 || !p2) {
    showError("resetMsg2", "Fill all fields");
    return;
  }
  if (p1 !== p2) {
    showError("resetMsg2", "Passwords don't match");
    return;
  }
  if (p1.length < 4) {
    showError("resetMsg2", "Password too short");
    return;
  }
  
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = "Verifying...";
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = "Verify & Reset";
      if (res.success) {
        alert(res.message);
        closeReset();
      } else {
        showError("resetMsg2", res.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = "Verify & Reset";
      showError("resetMsg2", "Error: " + err.message);
    })
    .verifyOTPAndResetPassword(uid, otp, p1);
}

function openChangePassword() {
  document.getElementById("changePasswordModal").style.display = "flex";
  document.getElementById("changeOldPass").value = "";
  document.getElementById("changeNewPass1").value = "";
  document.getElementById("changeNewPass2").value = "";
  hideError("changePassMsg");
  closeSidebar();
}
// ✅ NEW: Sab roles ke liye ek hi modal use karo
function openChangePasswordForRole() {
  // Existing member modal hi reuse karo
  openChangePassword();
  closeSidebar();
}
function closeChangePassword() {
  document.getElementById("changePasswordModal").style.display = "none";
}

function changePassword() {
  const oldPass = document.getElementById("changeOldPass").value;
  const newPass1 = document.getElementById("changeNewPass1").value;
  const newPass2 = document.getElementById("changeNewPass2").value;
  const btn = document.getElementById("changePassBtn");
  
  hideError("changePassMsg");
  
  if (!oldPass || !newPass1 || !newPass2) {
    showError("changePassMsg", "Fill all fields");
    return;
  }
  
  // ✅ FIX M-1: Client-side password comparison hataya — server pe verify hoga
  // oldPass ab changePasswordWithVerify() ko bheja jayega jo backend pe verify karega
  
  if (newPass1 !== newPass2) {
    showError("changePassMsg", "New passwords don't match");
    return;
  }
  
  if (newPass1.length < 4) {
    showError("changePassMsg", "Password too short");
    return;
  }
  
  if (oldPass === newPass1) {
    showError("changePassMsg", "New password must be different");
    return;
  }
  
  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = "Changing...";
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = "Change Password";
      if (res.success) {
        // ✅ FIX M-1: Password memory mein update nahi karte
        alert("Password changed successfully!");
        closeChangePassword();
        // Clear input fields
        document.getElementById("changeOldPass").value = "";
        document.getElementById("changeNewPass1").value = "";
        document.getElementById("changeNewPass2").value = "";
      } else {
        showError("changePassMsg", res.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = "Change Password";
      showError("changePassMsg", "Error: " + err.message);
    })
    .changePasswordWithOldVerify(currentUserId, oldPass, newPass1, currentUserToken);
}

// ── Member: Request Submit ────────────────────────────────────
function openRequestModal() {
  document.getElementById('reqModal').style.display = 'flex';
  document.getElementById('reqType').value = '';
  document.getElementById('reqUserId').value = currentUserId;
  document.getElementById('reqDate').value = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-GB');
  document.getElementById('reqLoanFields').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('reqComplaintField').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('reqMsg').textContent = '';
  document.getElementById('reqMsg').style.display = 'none';
  closeSidebar && closeSidebar();
}

function closeRequestModal() {
  document.getElementById('reqModal').style.display = 'none';
}

function onReqTypeChange() {
  var type = document.getElementById('reqType').value;
  document.getElementById('reqLoanFields').style.display    = (type === 'Loan Request')          ? 'block' : 'none';
  document.getElementById('reqComplaintField').style.display = (type === 'Complaint & Feedback')  ? 'block' : 'none';
}

function submitRequest() {
  var type    = document.getElementById('reqType').value;
  var btn     = document.getElementById('reqSubmitBtn');
  var msgDiv  = document.getElementById('reqMsg');

  msgDiv.style.display = 'none';

  if (!type) {
    msgDiv.textContent = '⚠️ Please select request type';
    msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
    return;
  }

  var requestData = {
    userId:     currentUserId,
    type:       type,
    branchCode: sessionStorage.getItem('memberBranchCode') || ''
  };

  if (type === 'Loan Request') {
    var amt    = document.getElementById('reqAmount').value;
    var scheme = document.getElementById('reqScheme').value;
    if (!amt || !scheme) {
      msgDiv.textContent = '⚠️ Fill amount and scheme';
      msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
      return;
    }
    requestData.amount  = amt;
    requestData.scheme  = scheme;
    requestData.details = 'Loan Request: ₹' + amt + ' | ' + scheme;
  } else {
    var details = document.getElementById('reqDetails').value.trim();
    if (!details) {
      msgDiv.textContent = '⚠️ Enter details';
      msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
      return;
    }
    requestData.details = details;
  }

  btn.disabled = true;
  btn.textContent = 'Submitting...';

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'Submit Request';
      if (res.success) {
        closeRequestModal();
        alert('✅ Request submitted successfully!\nRequest ID: ' + (res.requestId || ''));
      } else {
        msgDiv.textContent = '❌ ' + res.message;
        msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      btn.disabled = false;
      btn.textContent = 'Submit Request';
      msgDiv.textContent = '❌ Error: ' + err.message;
      msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
    })
    .submitRequest(requestData);
}

// ── Member: View My Requests ──────────────────────────────────
function viewMyRequests() {
  document.getElementById('myReqModal').style.display = 'flex';
  var list = document.getElementById('myReqList');
  list.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;"><div class="spinner" style="margin:0 auto 10px;"></div><p>Loading...</p></div>';
  closeSidebar && closeSidebar();

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.success) {
        renderMyRequests(res.requests || []);
      } else {
        list.innerHTML = '<p style="color:red;padding:20px;text-align:center;">❌ ' + escapeHtml(res.message) + '</p>';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      list.innerHTML = '<p style="color:red;padding:20px;text-align:center;">❌ ' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</p>';
    })
    .getUserRequests(currentUserId);
}

function closeMyRequests() {
  document.getElementById('myReqModal').style.display = 'none';
}

function renderMyRequests(requests) {
  var list = document.getElementById('myReqList');
  if (!requests.length) {
    list.innerHTML = '<p style="text-align:center;color:#666;padding:20px;">No requests found.</p>';
    return;
  }

  var statusColors = {
    'Pending':      '#f39c12',
    'UNDER REVIEW': '#3498db',
    'APPROVED':     '#27ae60',
    'CLOSED':       '#95a5a6',
    'REJECTED':     '#e74c3c'
  };

  var html = '';
  requests.forEach(function(r) {
    var color = statusColors[r.status] || '#7f8c8d';
    var statusBadge = '<span style="background:' + color + ';color:#fff;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:12px;font-size:11px;font-weight:bold;">' + r.status + '</span>';
    html += '<div style="background:#f8f9fa;border-radius:10px;padding:14px;margin-bottom:12px;border-left:4px solid ' + color + ';">' +
      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:8px;">' +
        '<strong style="color:#2c3e50;">' + r.type + '</strong>' +
        statusBadge +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="font-size:13px;color:#555;margin-bottom:6px;">' + (r.details || '') + '</div>' +
      (r.amount ? '<div style="font-size:13px;"><strong>Amount:</strong> ₹' + r.amount + (r.scheme ? ' | ' + r.scheme : '') + '</div>' : '') +
      (r.comment ? '<div style="font-size:12px;color:#2980b9;margin-top:6px;">💬 Supervisor: ' + r.comment + '</div>' : '') +
      '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#999;margin-top:6px;">📅 ' + r.date + (r.updatedOn ? ' | Updated: ' + r.updatedOn : '') + '</div>' +
    '</div>';
  });
  list.innerHTML = html;
}

function addRequestSearch() {
  const input = document.getElementById('requestSearchInput');
  const table = document.getElementById('requestsTable');
  
  if (!input || !table) return;
  
  input.addEventListener('keyup', function() {
    const filter = this.value.toUpperCase();
    const rows = table.getElementsByTagName('tr');
    
    for (let i = 1; i < rows.length; i++) {
      const txtValue = rows[i].textContent || rows[i].innerText;
      if (txtValue.toUpperCase().indexOf(filter) > -1) {
        rows[i].style.display = '';
      } else {
        rows[i].style.display = 'none';
      }
    }
  });
}

function openRequestUpdateModal(rowIndex, userId, type, currentStatus, currentNotes) {
  let modal = document.getElementById('requestUpdateModal');
  
  if (!modal) {
    modal = document.createElement('div');
    modal.id = 'requestUpdateModal';
    modal.className = 'modal';
    modal.innerHTML = `
      <div class="modal-content">
        <h3>📝 Update Member Request</h3>
        
        <div style="background: rgba(255,255,255,0.05); padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin-bottom: 20px;">
          <div style="color: white; margin-bottom: 8px;">
            <strong style="color: #FFD700;">User ID:</strong> <span id="modalUserId"></span>
          </div>
          <div style="color: white;">
            <strong style="color: #FFD700;">Request Type:</strong> <span id="modalRequestType"></span>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="form-group">
          <label style="color: #28a745; font-weight: bold;">📊 Status</label>
          <select id="modalRequestStatus" style="width:100%; padding:12px; border:2px solid #28a745;">
            <option value="">-- Select Status --</option>
            <option value="Pending">⏳ Pending</option>
            <option value="Approved">✅ Approved</option>
            <option value="Rejected">❌ Rejected</option>
            <option value="In Progress">🔄 In Progress</option>
            <option value="Under Review">🔍 Under Review</option>
            <option value="Closed">🔒 Closed</option>
          </select>
        </div>
        
        <div class="form-group">
          <label style="color: #007bff; font-weight: bold;">💬 Supervisor Comments / Remarks</label>
          <textarea id="modalRequestNotes" rows="4" placeholder="Add comments, remarks, or additional information..." style="width:100%; padding:12px; border:2px solid #ddd; resize:vertical;"></textarea>
        </div>
        
        <div id="modalRequestMsg" class="error"></div>
        
        <button onclick="saveRequestUpdate()" style="background:#28a745; color:white; width:100%; padding:15px; border:none; border-radius:8px; font-size:16px; cursor:pointer; font-weight: bold;">
          💾 Update Request
        </button>
        <button onclick="closeRequestUpdateModal()" class="btn-secondary" style="margin-top: 10px; width:100%; padding:12px;">
          Cancel
        </button>
      </div>
    `;
    document.body.appendChild(modal);
  }
  
  // Store rowIndex globally
  window.currentRequestRowIndex = rowIndex;
  
  // Populate modal
  document.getElementById('modalUserId').textContent = userId;
  document.getElementById('modalRequestType').textContent = type;
  document.getElementById('modalRequestStatus').value = currentStatus;
  document.getElementById('modalRequestNotes').value = currentNotes;
  
  modal.style.display = 'flex';
}

function closeRequestUpdateModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('requestUpdateModal');
  if (modal) modal.style.display = 'none';
}

function saveRequestUpdate() {
  const status = document.getElementById('modalRequestStatus').value;
  const notes = document.getElementById('modalRequestNotes').value.trim();
  const msgDiv = document.getElementById('modalRequestMsg');
  
  if (!status) {
    msgDiv.innerHTML = '⚠️ Please select a status';
    msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
    msgDiv.style.color = '#dc3545';
    return;
  }
  
  msgDiv.innerHTML = '⏳ Updating request...';
  msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
  msgDiv.style.color = '#007bff';
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result.success) {
        msgDiv.innerHTML = '✅ Request updated successfully!';
        msgDiv.style.color = '#28a745';
        
        setTimeout(() => {
          closeRequestUpdateModal();
          loadMemberRequests(); // Refresh list
        }, 1500);
      } else {
        msgDiv.innerHTML = '❌ Error: ' + escapeHtml(result.message);
        msgDiv.style.color = '#dc3545';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      msgDiv.innerHTML = '❌ Error: ' + escapeHtml(error.message);
      msgDiv.style.color = '#dc3545';
    })
    .approveMemberRequest(window.currentRequestRowIndex, status, notes);
}


// ============================================
// PRINT STATEMENT
// ============================================
function printDepositStatement() {
  closeSidebar();
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.success) {
        generatePrintContent(res);
        window.print();
      } else {
        alert("Error: " + res.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      alert("Error: " + err.message);
    })
    .generateDepositStatement(currentUserId);
}

function generatePrintContent(data) {
  var html = '<table style="width:100%;margin-bottom:20px;">';
  html += '<tr><th colspan="2" style="background:#c62828;color:white;">Member Information</th></tr>';
  html += '<tr><th>Member ID:</th><td>' + data.profile.memberId + '</td></tr>';
  html += '<tr><th>Name:</th><td>' + data.profile.name + '</td></tr>';
  html += '<tr><th>Account No:</th><td>' + data.profile.accountNo + '</td></tr>';
  html += '<tr><th>Email:</th><td>' + data.profile.email + '</td></tr>';
  html += '</table><h3>Deposit Statement</h3>';
  
  if (data.deposits.length > 0) {
    html += '<table><tr><th>Account</th><th>Amount</th><th>Interest</th><th>Balance</th><th>Date</th><th>Month</th></tr>';
    for (var i = 0; i < data.deposits.length; i++) {
      var d = data.deposits[i];
      html += '<tr>';
      html += '<td>' + d.accountNo + '</td>';
      html += '<td>' + d.amount + '</td>';
      html += '<td>' + d.interest + '</td>';
      html += '<td>' + d.currentBalance + '</td>';
      html += '<td>' + d.date + '</td>';
      html += '<td>' + d.monthFor + '</td>';
      html += '</tr>';
    }
    html += '</table>';
  } else {
    html += '<p>No deposits found.</p>';
  }
  
  html += '<p style="margin-top:30px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;">Generated: ' + data.generatedDate + '</p>';
  document.getElementById("printContent").innerHTML = html;
}

// ============================================
// CALCULATOR FUNCTIONS
// ============================================
function calculateSIP() {
  const amount = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sipAmount').value);
  const rate = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sipRate').value);
  const years = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sipYears').value);
  const resultDiv = document.getElementById('sipResult');

  if (!amount || !rate || !years) {
    resultDiv.style.display = 'block';
    resultDiv.textContent = 'Please fill all fields correctly.';
    return;
  }

  const n = years * 12;
  const r = rate / 12 / 100;
  const futureValue = amount * ((Math.pow(1 + r, n) - 1) / r) * (1 + r);
  const invested = amount * n;
  const gain = futureValue - invested;

  resultDiv.style.display = 'block';
  resultDiv.innerHTML =
    'Total Invested: ₹' + invested.toFixed(0) +
    '<br>Estimated Value: ₹' + futureValue.toFixed(0) +
    '<br>Estimated Gain: ₹' + gain.toFixed(0);
}

function calculateLumpsum() {
  const amount = parseFloat(document.getElementById('lumpAmount').value);
  const rate = parseFloat(document.getElementById('lumpRate').value);
  const years = parseFloat(document.getElementById('lumpYears').value);
  const resultDiv = document.getElementById('lumpResult');

  if (!amount || !rate || !years) {
    resultDiv.style.display = 'block';
    resultDiv.textContent = 'Please fill all fields correctly.';
    return;
  }

  const r = rate / 100;
  const futureValue = amount * Math.pow(1 + r, years);
  const gain = futureValue - amount;

  resultDiv.style.display = 'block';
  resultDiv.innerHTML =
    'Initial Investment: ₹' + amount.toFixed(0) +
    '<br>Estimated Value: ₹' + futureValue.toFixed(0) +
    '<br>Estimated Gain: ₹' + gain.toFixed(0);
}

function calculateLoanEMI() {
  const principal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('loanCalcAmount').value);
  const rate = parseFloat(document.getElementById('loanCalcRate').value);
  const months = parseFloat(document.getElementById('loanCalcMonths').value);
  const resultDiv = document.getElementById('loanCalcResult');

  if (!principal || !rate || !months) {
    resultDiv.style.display = 'block';
    resultDiv.textContent = 'Please fill all fields correctly.';
    return;
  }

  const r = rate / 12 / 100;
  const emi = principal * r * Math.pow(1 + r, months) / (Math.pow(1 + r, months) - 1);
  const totalPayable = emi * months;
  const interestPayable = totalPayable - principal;

  resultDiv.style.display = 'block';
  resultDiv.innerHTML =
    'Monthly EMI: ₹' + emi.toFixed(0) +
    '<br>Total Interest: ₹' + interestPayable.toFixed(0) +
    '<br>Total Amount Payable: ₹' + totalPayable.toFixed(0);
}

function calculateGoalSIP() {
  const goal = parseFloat(document.getElementById('goalAmount').value);
  const years = parseFloat(document.getElementById('goalYears').value);
  const rate = parseFloat(document.getElementById('goalRate').value);
  const resultDiv = document.getElementById('goalResult');

  if (!goal || !rate || !years) {
    resultDiv.style.display = 'block';
    resultDiv.textContent = 'Please fill all fields correctly.';
    return;
  }

  const n = years * 12;
  const r = rate / 12 / 100;
  const factor = (Math.pow(1 + r, n) - 1) * (1 + r) / r;
  const sip = goal / factor;

  resultDiv.style.display = 'block';
  resultDiv.innerHTML =
    'Required Monthly SIP: ₹' + sip.toFixed(0) +
    '<br>To reach goal of ₹' + goal.toFixed(0) +
    ' in ' + years + ' years (approx).';
}

// ============================================
// NOTIFICATIONS
// ============================================
function checkNotifications() {
  if (!currentUserId) return;
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      if (res.success && res.notifications && res.notifications.length > 0) {
        showNotificationPopup(res.notifications);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      console.error('Notification check error:', err);
    })
    .getNotifications(currentUserId);
}

function showNotificationPopup(notifications) {
  var modal = document.getElementById('notificationModal');
  if (!modal) {
    modal = document.createElement('div');
    modal.id = 'notificationModal';
    modal.className = 'modal';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    modal.innerHTML = `
      <div class="modal-content" style="max-width: 500px;">
        <h3 style="color: #FFD700; margin-bottom: 20px;">🔔 New Notifications</h3>
        <div id="notificationList"></div>
        <button class="btn-primary" onclick="closeNotifications()" style="margin-top: 20px; width: 100%;">OK, Got it!</button>
      </div>
    `;
    document.body.appendChild(modal);
  } else {
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  }
  
  var listDiv = document.getElementById('notificationList');
  var html = '';
  
  for (var i = 0; i < notifications.length; i++) {
    var notif = notifications[i];
    var icon = '🔔';
    if (notif.type === 'APPROVAL') icon = '✅';
    if (notif.type === 'REJECTION') icon = '❌';
    if (notif.message.indexOf('Approved') >= 0) icon = '✅';
    if (notif.message.indexOf('Rejected') >= 0) icon = '❌';
    
    html += '<div style="background: rgba(255,255,255,0.1); padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin-bottom: 10px; border-left: 3px solid #FFD700;">';
    html += '<div style="display: flex; align-items: center; margin-bottom: 8px;">';
    html += '<spanstyle="font-size: 24px; margin-right: 10px;">' + icon + '</span>';
html += '<div style="flex: 1;">';
html += '<div style="color: white; font-weight: bold; font-size: 14px;">' + escapeHtml(notif.message) + '</div>'; // ✅ XSS fix
html += '<div style="color: rgba(255,255,255,0.7); font-size: 12px; margin-top: 3px;">' + escapeHtml(notif.date) + '</div>'; // ✅ XSS fix
html += '</div>';
html += '</div>';
html += '</div>';
}
listDiv.innerHTML = html;
}
function closeNotifications() {
var modal = document.getElementById('notificationModal');
if (modal) {
modal.style.display = 'none';
}
google.script.run
.withSuccessHandler(function() {
console.log('Notifications marked as read');
})
.markAllNotificationsRead(currentUserId);
}
function checkNotificationsAfterLogin() {
setTimeout(function() {
checkNotifications();
}, 2000);
}
// ============================================
// EVENT LISTENERS
// ============================================
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  // Password field enter key listeners
  const passwordField = document.getElementById("password");
  if (passwordField) {
    passwordField.addEventListener("keypress", function(e) {
      if (e.key === "Enter") attemptLogin();
    });
  }
  
  const operatorPasswordField = document.getElementById("operatorPassword");
  if (operatorPasswordField) {
    operatorPasswordField.addEventListener("keypress", function(e) {
      if (e.key === "Enter") attemptOperatorLogin();
    });
  }
  
  const supervisorPasswordField = document.getElementById("supervisorPassword");
  if (supervisorPasswordField) {
    supervisorPasswordField.addEventListener("keypress", function(e) {
      if (e.key === "Enter") attemptSupervisorLogin();
    });
  }
  
  // ✅ ADDED - Check and restore supervisor session on page load
  const supervisorId = sessionStorage.getItem('supervisorId');
  const branchCode = sessionStorage.getItem('branchCode');
  const supervisorDashboard = document.getElementById('supervisorDashboard');
  
  if (supervisorId && branchCode && supervisorDashboard && !supervisorDashboard.classList.contains('hidden')) {
    // Supervisor dashboard is visible, verify and update day status
    const storedDayStatus = sessionStorage.getItem('dayStatus') || 'CLOSED';
    
    // Update UI immediately with stored status
    updateDayStatusUI(storedDayStatus);
    
    // Then verify with backend and update if different
    google.script.run
      .withSuccessHandler(function(response) {
        if (response.success) {
          const actualStatus = response.dayStatus || 'CLOSED';
          
          // Update session if different
          if (actualStatus !== storedDayStatus) {
            sessionStorage.setItem('dayStatus', actualStatus);
          }
          
          // Update UI with actual status
          updateDayStatusUI(actualStatus);
        }
      })
      .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
        console.log('Failed to verify day status:', error);
      })
      .getSupervisorDayStatus(branchCode);
  }
});

const manifestData = {
"name": "DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION Member Portal",
"short_name": "DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION",
"start_url": ".",
"display": "standalone",
"background_color": "#c62828",
"theme_color": "#c62828",
"icons": [{
"src": "data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg' viewBox='0 0 192 192'%3E%3Crect fill='%23c62828' width='192' height='192' rx='40'/%3E%3Ctext x='96' y='135' font-size='100' text-anchor='middle' fill='white' font-family='Arial' font-weight='bold'%3EFL%3C/text%3E%3C/svg%3E",
"sizes": "192x192",
"type": "image/svg+xml"
}]
};
const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(manifestData)], {type: 'application/json'});
const manifestURL = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
const link = document.createElement('link');
link.rel = 'manifest';
link.href = manifestURL;
document.head.appendChild(link);
if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
window.addEventListener('load', () => {
const swCode = self.addEventListener('install', () => self.skipWaiting()); self.addEventListener('activate', e => e.waitUntil(self.clients.claim())); self.addEventListener('fetch', e => e.respondWith(fetch(e.request).catch(() => caches.match(e.request))));;
const swBlob = new Blob([swCode], {type: 'application/javascript'});
const swUrl = URL.createObjectURL(swBlob);
navigator.serviceWorker.register(swUrl).then(() => console.log('✅ PWA Ready'));
});
}
console.log('✅ All scripts loaded successfully!');

// 📖 PASSBOOK & TRANSACTION RECEIPT

/**
 * Generate and display passbook
 */
function generatePassbook() {
  const accountNo = prompt('Enter Account Number:');
  if (!accountNo || !accountNo.trim()) return;

  showLoading('Generating passbook...');

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideLoading();
      if (result.success) {
        // ✅ FIX: currentBalance backend se aata hai ab
        displayPassbook(result.account, result.transactions, result.currentBalance);
      } else {
        _showSuccessModal('❌ Error', result.message, '#e74c3c');
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoading();
      _showSuccessModal('❌ Server Error', error.message, '#e74c3c');
    })
    .generatePassbook(accountNo.trim());
}
/**
 * Display passbook in modal
 */
function displayPassbook(account, transactions, currentBalance) {
  var bal = parseFloat(currentBalance) || 0;

  var html =
    '<div style="max-width:800px;margin:20px auto;background:white;padding:30px;border-radius:10px;" id="passbookPrintContent">' +

      // Header
      '<div style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:25px;border-bottom:3px solid #5B4B8A;padding-bottom:15px;">' +
        '<h2 style="color:#5B4B8A;margin:0;">DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION</h2>' +
        '<h3 style="color:#764BA2;margin:8px 0 0 0;">PASSBOOK</h3>' +
      '</div>' +

      // Account Info
      '<div style="background:#f8f9fa;padding:20px;border-radius:8px;margin-bottom:25px;">' +
        '<table style="width:100%;border:none;">' +
          '<tr><td style="border:none;padding:6px;width:40%;"><strong>Account No:</strong></td>' +
               '<td style="border:none;padding:6px;">' + (account.accountNo || '') + '</td></tr>' +
          '<tr><td style="border:none;padding:6px;"><strong>Member ID:</strong></td>' +
               '<td style="border:none;padding:6px;">' + (account.memberId || '') + '</td></tr>' +
          '<tr><td style="border:none;padding:6px;"><strong>Account Holder:</strong></td>' +
               '<td style="border:none;padding:6px;">' + (account.name || '') + '</td></tr>' +
          '<tr><td style="border:none;padding:6px;"><strong>Account Type:</strong></td>' +
               '<td style="border:none;padding:6px;">' + (account.accountType || '') + '</td></tr>' +
          '<tr><td style="border:none;padding:6px;"><strong>Open Date:</strong></td>' +
               '<td style="border:none;padding:6px;">' + (account.openDate || '') + '</td></tr>' +
          '<tr><td style="border:none;padding:6px;"><strong>Status:</strong></td>' +
               '<td style="border:none;padding:6px;">' + (account.status || '') + '</td></tr>' +
          '<tr><td style="border:none;padding:6px;"><strong>Current Balance:</strong></td>' +
               '<td style="border:none;padding:6px;"><strong style="color:#27ae60;font-size:18px;">₹' + bal.toLocaleString('en-IN', {minimumFractionDigits:2}) + '</strong></td></tr>' +
        '</table>' +
      '</div>' +

      // Transactions table
      '<h4 style="color:#5B4B8A;margin-bottom:15px;">Transaction History (' + (transactions ? transactions.length : 0) + ' entries)</h4>' +
      '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:13px;">' +
        '<thead>' +
          '<tr style="background:#5B4B8A;color:white;">' +
            '<th style="padding:10px;text-align:left;border:1px solid #ddd;">Date</th>' +
            '<th style="padding:10px;text-align:left;border:1px solid #ddd;">Month For</th>' +
            '<th style="padding:10px;text-align:right;border:1px solid #ddd;">Amount</th>' +
            '<th style="padding:10px;text-align:right;border:1px solid #ddd;">Interest</th>' +
            '<th style="padding:10px;text-align:right;border:1px solid #ddd;">Balance</th>' +
          '</tr>' +
        '</thead>' +
        '<tbody>';

  if (!transactions || transactions.length === 0) {
    html += '<tr><td colspan="5" style="padding:20px;text-align:center;color:#666;border:1px solid #ddd;">No transactions found</td></tr>';
  } else {
    transactions.forEach(function(txn) {
      var amt  = parseFloat(txn.amount)   || 0;
      var intr = parseFloat(txn.interest) || 0;
      var bal2 = parseFloat(txn.balance)  || 0;
      html +=
        '<tr>' +
          '<td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;">'  + (txn.date    || '') + '</td>' +
          '<td style="padding:8px;border:1px solid #ddd;">'  + (txn.monthFor || '') + '</td>' +
          '<td style="padding:8px;text-align:right;border:1px solid #ddd;">₹' + amt.toLocaleString('en-IN',{minimumFractionDigits:2})  + '</td>' +
          '<td style="padding:8px;text-align:right;border:1px solid #ddd;">₹' + intr.toLocaleString('en-IN',{minimumFractionDigits:2}) + '</td>' +
          '<td style="padding:8px;text-align:right;border:1px solid #ddd;font-weight:bold;">₹' + bal2.toLocaleString('en-IN',{minimumFractionDigits:2}) + '</td>' +
        '</tr>';
    });
  }

  html +=
        '</tbody>' +
      '</table>' +

      // ✅ FIX 4: Print button — window.print() ki jagah printPassbookContent() use karo
      '<div style="margin-top:25px;text-align:center;display:flex;gap:10px;justify-content:center;" class="no-print">' +
        '<button onclick="printPassbookContent()" style="background:#5B4B8A;color:white;padding:12px 30px;border:none;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:15px;">' +
          '🖨️ Print Passbook' +
        '</button>' +
        '<button onclick="closePassbookModal()" style="background:#6c757d;color:white;padding:12px 30px;border:none;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:15px;">' +
          'Close' +
        '</button>' +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>';

  var modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'passbookModal';
  modal.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.8);z-index:10000;overflow-y:auto;padding:20px;';
  modal.innerHTML = html;
  document.body.appendChild(modal);
}
// ✅ FIX 4: GAS iFrame-safe print function
function printPassbookContent() {
  var content = document.getElementById('passbookPrintContent');
  if (!content) return;

  var printWindow = window.open('', '_blank');
  printWindow.document.write(
    '<html><head><title>Passbook</title>' +
    '<style>body{font-family:Arial,sans-serif;margin:20px;}table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;}' +
    'th,td{border:1px solid #ddd;padding:8px;}th{background:#5B4B8A;color:white;}</style>' +
    '</head><body>' +
    content.innerHTML +
    '</body></html>'
  );
  printWindow.document.close();
  printWindow.focus();
  setTimeout(function() { printWindow.print(); printWindow.close(); }, 500);
}

/**
 * Close passbook modal
 */
function closePassbookModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('passbookModal');
  if (modal) {
    modal.remove();
  }
}

/**
 * Generate transaction receipt
 */
function generateReceipt(transactionId) {
  if (!transactionId) {
    transactionId = prompt('Enter Transaction ID:');
  }
  
  if (!transactionId) return;
  
  showLoading('Generating receipt...');
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideLoading();
      
      if (result.success) {
        displayReceipt(result.transaction);
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoading();
      alert('Error: ' + error.message);
    })
    .generateTransactionReceipt(transactionId);
}

/**
 * Display transaction receipt
 */
function displayReceipt(txn) {
  const date = new Date(txn.date);
  const dateStr = date.toLocaleDateString('en-IN');
  const timeStr = date.toLocaleTimeString('en-IN');
  
  let html = `
    <div style="max-width: 500px; margin: 20px auto; background: white; padding: 30px; border-radius: 10px; border: 2px dashed #5B4B8A;">
      <div style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 25px;">
        <h2 style="color: #5B4B8A; margin: 0;">TRANSACTION RECEIPT</h2>
        <p style="color: #666; font-size: 14px; margin: 5px 0;">DUMMY NAME ORGANIZATION</p>
      </div>
      
      <div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 20px; border-radius: 8px; margin-bottom: 20px;">
        <table style="width: 100%; border: none;">
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; color: #666;">Transaction ID:</td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; font-weight: bold;">${txn.id}</td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; color: #666;">Account Number:</td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; font-weight: bold;">${txn.accountNo}</td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; color: #666;">Date:</td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; font-weight: bold;">${dateStr}</td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; color: #666;">Time:</td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; font-weight: bold;">${timeStr}</td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; color: #666;">Type:</td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;">
              <span style="background: ${txn.type === 'DEPOSIT' ? '#d4edda' : '#fff3cd'}; 
                           color: ${txn.type === 'DEPOSIT' ? '#155724' : '#856404'}; 
                           padding: 4px 12px; border-radius: 4px; font-weight: bold;">
                ${txn.type}
              </span>
            </td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; color: #666;">Amount:</td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;">
              <span style="font-size: 24px; font-weight: bold; color: #5B4B8A;">₹${Number(txn.amount).toFixed(2)}</span>
            </td>
          </tr>
          ${txn.remarks ? `
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px; color: #666;">Remarks:</td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;">${txn.remarks}</td>
          </tr>
          ` : ''}
        </table>
      </div>
      
      <div style="text-align: center; font-size: 12px; color: #999; margin-top: 20px; padding-top: 15px; border-top: 1px dashed #ddd;">
        This is a computer-generated receipt
      </div>
      
      <div style="margin-top: 25px; text-align: center;">
        <button onclick="window.print()" style="background: #5B4B8A; color: white; padding: 12px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 15px; margin-right: 10px;">
          🖨️ Print Receipt
        </button>
        <button onclick="closeReceiptModal()" style="background: #6c757d; color: white; padding: 12px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 15px;">
          Close
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
  
  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'receiptModal';
  modal.style.cssText = 'position: fixed; top: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.8); z-index: 10000; overflow-y: auto; padding: 20px;';
  modal.innerHTML = html;
  
  document.body.appendChild(modal);
}

/**
 * Close receipt modal
 */
function closeReceiptModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('receiptModal');
  if (modal) {
    modal.remove();
  }
}

// ── DAILY SCHEME-WISE REPORT (Reports Menu se) ───────────────────
function showDailySchemeWiseReport() {
  closeReportsMenu();

  var modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'dailySchemeReportModal';
  modal.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.85);z-index:10000;overflow-y:auto;padding:20px;box-sizing:border-box;';

  var today = new Date();
  var todayStr = today.getFullYear() + '-' +
    String(today.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0') + '-' +
    String(today.getDate()).padStart(2,'0');

  modal.innerHTML =
    '<div style="max-width:800px;margin:20px auto;background:white;border-radius:15px;overflow:hidden;">' +
      '<div style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,#f093fb,#f5576c);padding:20px 24px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;">' +
        '<div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.8);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;">Reports</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:bold;color:white;margin-top:2px;">🏷️ Scheme-Wise Daily Report</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<button onclick="document.getElementById(\'dailySchemeReportModal\').remove()" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.2);color:white;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.4);padding:8px 16px;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;font-weight:bold;">✖ Close</button>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="padding:20px 24px;background:#f8f8f8;display:flex;gap:12px;align-items:center;flex-wrap:wrap;">' +
        '<div style="flex:1;min-width:180px;">' +
          '<label style="font-size:12px;color:#666;display:block;margin-bottom:5px;">Date</label>' +
          '<input type="date" id="dsrDate" value="' + todayStr + '" style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:1px solid #ddd;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box;">' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div style="padding-top:22px;">' +
          '<button onclick="loadDailySchemeWiseReport()" style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,#f093fb,#f5576c);color:white;border:none;padding:11px 24px;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;">📊 Generate</button>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div id="dsrContent" style="padding:20px 24px;"><div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:#999;">Date select karke Generate dabayein</div></div>' +
    '</div>';

  document.body.appendChild(modal);
}

function loadDailySchemeWiseReport() {
  var dateVal = document.getElementById('dsrDate') ? document.getElementById('dsrDate').value : '';
  var reportDateStr = '';
  if (dateVal && dateVal.trim()) {
    var parts = dateVal.split('-');
    if (parts.length === 3) reportDateStr = parts[2] + '/' + parts[1] + '/' + parts[0];
  }

  var container = document.getElementById('dsrContent');
  if (!container) return;
  container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;"><div style="font-size:36px;margin-bottom:10px;">⏳</div><p style="color:#888;">Report generate ho raha hai...</p></div>';

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (!result || !result.success) {
        container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#e74c3c;">❌ ' + escapeHtml(result ? result.message : 'Unknown error') + '</div>';
        return;
      }
      var fmt = function(n) {
        return '₹' + (parseFloat(n)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN', { minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2 });
      };
      container.innerHTML =
        '<div style="margin-bottom:12px;font-size:13px;color:#666;text-align:right;">📅 ' + result.reportDate + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; Branch: <b>' + result.branchCode + '</b></div>' +
        '<button onclick="window.print()" class="no-print" style="background:#5B4B8A;color:white;border:none;padding:8px 18px;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:16px;">🖨️ Print</button>' +
        _schemeReportHTML(result, fmt);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#e74c3c;">❌ ' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</div>';
    })
    .getBranchDailyReport(currentUserId, reportDateStr);
}

// ── DAILY OPERATOR-WISE REPORT (Reports Menu se) ─────────────────
function showDailyOperatorWiseReport() {
  closeReportsMenu();

  var modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'dailyOperatorReportModal';
  modal.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.85);z-index:10000;overflow-y:auto;padding:20px;box-sizing:border-box;';

  var today = new Date();
  var todayStr = today.getFullYear() + '-' +
    String(today.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0') + '-' +
    String(today.getDate()).padStart(2,'0');

  modal.innerHTML =
    '<div style="max-width:900px;margin:20px auto;background:white;border-radius:15px;overflow:hidden;">' +
      '<div style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,#43e97b,#38f9d7);padding:20px 24px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;">' +
        '<div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(0,0,0,0.5);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;">Reports</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:bold;color:#1a472a;margin-top:2px;">👤 Operator-Wise Daily Report</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<button onclick="document.getElementById(\'dailyOperatorReportModal\').remove()" style="background:rgba(0,0,0,0.1);color:#1a472a;border:1px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.2);padding:8px 16px;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;font-weight:bold;">✖ Close</button>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="padding:20px 24px;background:#f8f8f8;display:flex;gap:12px;align-items:center;flex-wrap:wrap;">' +
        '<div style="flex:1;min-width:180px;">' +
          '<label style="font-size:12px;color:#666;display:block;margin-bottom:5px;">Date</label>' +
          '<input type="date" id="dorDate" value="' + todayStr + '" style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:1px solid #ddd;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box;">' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div style="padding-top:22px;">' +
          '<button onclick="loadDailyOperatorWiseReport()" style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,#43e97b,#38f9d7);color:#1a472a;border:none;padding:11px 24px;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;">📊 Generate</button>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div id="dorContent" style="padding:20px 24px;"><div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:#999;">Date select karke Generate dabayein</div></div>' +
    '</div>';

  document.body.appendChild(modal);
}

function loadDailyOperatorWiseReport() {
  var dateVal = document.getElementById('dorDate') ? document.getElementById('dorDate').value : '';
  var reportDateStr = '';
  if (dateVal && dateVal.trim()) {
    var parts = dateVal.split('-');
    if (parts.length === 3) reportDateStr = parts[2] + '/' + parts[1] + '/' + parts[0];
  }

  var container = document.getElementById('dorContent');
  if (!container) return;
  container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;"><div style="font-size:36px;margin-bottom:10px;">⏳</div><p style="color:#888;">Report generate ho raha hai...</p></div>';

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (!result || !result.success) {
        container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#e74c3c;">❌ ' + escapeHtml(result ? result.message : 'Unknown error') + '</div>';
        return;
      }
      var fmt = function(n) {
        return '₹' + (parseFloat(n)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN', { minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2 });
      };
      container.innerHTML =
        '<div style="margin-bottom:12px;font-size:13px;color:#666;text-align:right;">📅 ' + result.reportDate + ' &nbsp;|&nbsp; Branch: <b>' + result.branchCode + '</b></div>' +
        '<button onclick="window.print()" class="no-print" style="background:#37474f;color:white;border:none;padding:8px 18px;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:16px;">🖨️ Print</button>' +
        _operatorReportHTML(result, fmt);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#e74c3c;">❌ ' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</div>';
    })
    .getBranchDailyReport(currentUserId, reportDateStr);
}

/**
 * Close reports menu
 */
function closeReportsMenu() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('reportsMenuModal');
  if (modal) modal.remove();
}

/**
 * Generate day end report
 */
function showDayEndReport() {
  closeReportsMenu();
  
  const date = prompt('Enter date (YYYY-MM-DD) or leave blank for today:');
  const reportDate = date || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  
  showLoading('Generating day end report...');
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideLoading();
      
      if (result.success) {
        displayDayEndReport(result.report);
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoading();
      alert('Error: ' + error.message);
    })
    .generateDayEndReport(dayBranchCache, reportDate);
}

          <div style="font-size: 13px; color: white; margin-bottom: 5px;">Net Collection</div>

/**
 * Show scheme-wise report
 */
function showSchemeWiseReport() {
  closeReportsMenu();
  
  const scheme = prompt('Enter scheme (SIP/LUMPSUM/FIXED) or leave blank for all:');
  
  showLoading('Generating scheme-wise report...');
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideLoading();
      
      if (result.success) {
        displaySchemeWiseReport(result);
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoading();
      alert('Error: ' + error.message);
    })
    .generateSchemeWiseReport(dayBranchCache, scheme);
}

/**
 * Display scheme-wise report
 */
function displaySchemeWiseReport(data) {
  let accountsHtml = '';
  
  if (data.accounts.length === 0) {
    accountsHtml = '<tr><td colspan="5" style="text-align: center; padding: 20px; color: #666;">No accounts found</td></tr>';
  } else {
    data.accounts.forEach(acc => {
      accountsHtml += `
        <tr>
          <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">${acc.accountNo}</td>
          <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">${acc.name}</td>
          <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">${acc.accountType}</td>
          <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">
            <span style="background: ${acc.status === 'ACTIVE' ? '#d4edda' : '#f8d7da'}; 
                         color: ${acc.status === 'ACTIVE' ? '#155724' : '#721c24'}; 
                         padding: 4px 10px; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 11px;">
              ${acc.status}
            </span>
          </td>
          <td style="padding: 10px; text-align: right; border: 1px solid #ddd;">₹${Number(acc.balance).toFixed(2)}</td>
        </tr>
      `;
    });
  }
  
  const html = `
    <div style="max-width: 900px; margin: 20px auto; background: white; padding: 30px; border-radius: 15px;">
      <div style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 30px; border-bottom: 3px solid #5B4B8A; padding-bottom: 20px;">
        <h2 style="color: #5B4B8A; margin: 0;">SCHEME-WISE REPORT</h2>
        <p style="color: #666; margin: 10px 0;">Branch: ${data.branchCode}</p>
        <p style="color: #666; margin: 5px 0;">Scheme: ${data.scheme}</p>
      </div>
      
      <div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 20px; border-radius: 10px; margin-bottom: 25px;">
        <div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr 1fr 1fr; gap: 15px; text-align: center;">
          <div>
            <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #666;">Total Accounts</div>
            <div style="font-size: 24px; font-weight: bold; color: #5B4B8A;">${data.totalAccounts}</div>
          </div>
          <div>
            <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #666;">Active</div>
            <div style="font-size: 24px; font-weight: bold; color: #28a745;">${data.activeAccounts}</div>
          </div>
          <div>
            <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #666;">Inactive</div>
            <div style="font-size: 24px; font-weight: bold; color: #dc3545;">${data.inactiveAccounts}</div>
          </div>
          <div>
            <div style="font-size: 12px; color: #666;">Total Balance</div>
            <div style="font-size: 24px; font-weight: bold; color: #5B4B8A;">₹${Number(data.totalBalance).toFixed(2)}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <h4 style="color: #5B4B8A; margin-bottom: 15px;">Account Details</h4>
      
      <div style="overflow-x: auto;">
        <table style="width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; font-size: 13px;">
          <thead>
            <tr style="background: #5B4B8A; color: white;">
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: left; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Account No</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: left; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Name</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: left; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Type</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: left; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Status</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: right; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Balance</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            ${accountsHtml}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
      
      <div style="margin-top: 30px; text-align: center;">
        <button onclick="window.print()" style="background: #5B4B8A; color: white; padding: 12px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 15px; margin-right: 10px;">
          🖨️ Print Report
        </button>
        <button onclick="closeSchemeReport()" style="background: #6c757d; color: white; padding: 12px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 15px;">
          Close
        </button>
      </div>

  `;
  
  const modal = document.createElement('div');

  document.body.appendChild(modal);
}

/**
 * Show customer statement
 */
function showCustomerStatement() {
  closeReportsMenu();

  // ✅ FIX: accountNo se statement — memberId nahi
  var accountNo = prompt('Enter Account Number:');
  if (!accountNo || !accountNo.trim()) return;

  showLoading('Generating customer statement...');

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideLoading();
      if (result.success) {
        displayCustomerStatement(result);
      } else {
        _showSuccessModal('❌ Error', result.message, '#e74c3c');
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoading();
      _showSuccessModal('❌ Error', error.message, '#e74c3c');
    })
    .generateCustomerStatement(accountNo.trim(), currentUserId);
}
/**
 * Display customer statement
 */
function displayCustomerStatement(data) {
  let txnHtml = '';
  
  if (data.transactions.length === 0) {
    txnHtml = '<tr><td colspan="5" style="text-align: center; padding: 20px; color: #666;">No transactions in this period</td></tr>';
  } else {
    data.transactions.forEach(txn => {
      const date = new Date(txn.date);
      const dateStr = date.toLocaleDateString('en-IN');
      
      txnHtml += `
        <tr>
          <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">${dateStr}</td>
          <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">${txn.id}</td>
          <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">
            <span style="background: ${txn.type === 'DEPOSIT' || txn.type === 'REPAYMENT' ? '#d4edda' : '#fff3cd'}; 
                         color: ${txn.type === 'DEPOSIT' || txn.type === 'REPAYMENT' ? '#155724' : '#856404'}; 
                         padding: 4px 10px; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 11px;">
              ${txn.type}
            </span>
          </td>
          <td style="padding: 10px; text-align: right; border: 1px solid #ddd;">₹${Number(txn.amount).toFixed(2)}</td>
          <td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">${txn.remarks || '-'}</td>
        </tr>
      `;
    });
  }
  
  const html = `
    <div style="max-width: 900px; margin: 20px auto; background: white; padding: 30px; border-radius: 15px;">
      <div style="text-align: center; margin-bottom: 30px; border-bottom: 3px solid #5B4B8A; padding-bottom: 20px;">
        <h2 style="color: #5B4B8A; margin: 0;">CUSTOMER STATEMENT</h2>
        <p style="color: #666; margin: 10px 0;">Period: ${new Date(data.fromDate).toLocaleDateString('en-IN')} to ${new Date(data.toDate).toLocaleDateString('en-IN')}</p>
      </div>
      
      <div style="background: #f8f9fa; padding: 20px; border-radius: 10px; margin-bottom: 25px;">
        <table style="width: 100%; border: none;">
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;"><strong>Account Number:</strong></td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;">${data.account.accountNo}</td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;"><strong>Account Holder:</strong></td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;">${data.account.name}</td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;"><strong>Account Type:</strong></td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;">${data.account.accountType}</td>
          </tr>
          <tr>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;"><strong>Current Balance:</strong></td>
            <td style="border: none; padding: 8px;"><strong>₹${Number(data.account.currentBalance).toFixed(2)}</strong></td>
          </tr>
        </table>
      </div>
      
      <h4 style="color: #5B4B8A; margin-bottom: 15px;">Transaction History (${data.totalTransactions} transactions)</h4>
      
      <div style="overflow-x: auto;">
        <table style="width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; font-size: 13px;">
          <thead>
            <tr style="background: #5B4B8A; color: white;">
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: left; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Date</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: left; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Transaction ID</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: left; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Type</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: right; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Amount</th>
              <th style="padding: 12px; text-align: left; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Remarks</th>
            </tr>
          </thead>
          <tbody>
            ${txnHtml}
          </tbody>
        </table>
      </div>
      
      <div style="margin-top: 30px; text-align: center;">
        <button onclick="window.print()" style="background: #5B4B8A; color: white; padding: 12px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 15px; margin-right: 10px;">
          🖨️ Print Statement
        </button>
        <button onclick="closeCustomerStatement()" style="background: #6c757d; color: white; padding: 12px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 15px;">
          Close
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
  
  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'customerStatementModal';
  modal.style.cssText = 'position: fixed; top: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.8); z-index: 10000; overflow-y: auto; padding: 20px;';
  modal.innerHTML = html;
  
  document.body.appendChild(modal);
}

 * Close customer statement

  const modal = document.getElementById('customerStatementModal');
  if (modal) modal.remove();

// 🖥️ OPERATOR COUNTER MANAGEMENT
// ============================================

/**
 * Close operator counter and return cash
 */
function closeCounter() {
  if (!confirm('Are you sure you want to close your counter? All cash will be returned to supervisor.')) {
    return;
  }
  
  showLoading('Closing counter...');
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideLoading();
      
      if (result.success) {
        alert(`✅ Counter closed successfully!\n\nCash returned: ₹${result.cashReturned}\n\nYou can now logout.`);
        
        // Reload operator data
        loadOperatorDetailsNew();
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoading();
      alert('Error: ' + error.message);
    })
    .closeOperatorCounter(currentUserId, currentSupervisorId);
}

/**
 * Show counter allocation modal (for supervisor)
 */
function showCounterAllocation() {
  const html = `
    <div style="max-width: 500px; margin: 20px auto; background: white; padding: 30px; border-radius: 15px;">
      <h2 style="color: #5B4B8A; margin-bottom: 25px; text-align: center;">🖥️ Allocate Counter</h2>
      
      <div class="form-group">
        <label><strong>Operator ID:</strong></label>
        <select id="allocOperatorId" style="width: 100%; padding: 12px; border: 2px solid #ddd; border-radius: 8px; margin-top: 8px; font-size: 16px;">
          <option value="">-- Loading operators... --</option>
        </select>
      </div>
      
      <div class="form-group" style="margin-top: 20px;">
        <label><strong>Counter Number:</strong></label>
        <input type="number" id="allocCounterNo" placeholder="e.g., 1, 2, 3" style="width: 100%; padding: 12px; border: 2px solid #ddd; border-radius: 8px; margin-top: 8px;">
      </div>
      
      <div style="margin-top: 30px; text-align: center;">
        <button onclick="submitCounterAllocation()" style="background: #5B4B8A; color: white; padding: 14px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; margin-right: 10px;">
          ✅ Allocate Counter
        </button>
        <button onclick="closeCounterAllocationModal()" style="background: #6c757d; color: white; padding: 14px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 16px;">
          Cancel
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
  
  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'counterAllocationModal';
  modal.style.cssText = 'position: fixed; top: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.8); z-index: 10000; overflow-y: auto; padding: 20px;';
  modal.innerHTML = html;
  
  document.body.appendChild(modal);
  
  // Load operators for dropdown
  loadOperatorsForDropdown('allocOperatorId');
}
/**
 * Submit counter allocation
 */
function submitCounterAllocation() {
  const operatorId = document.getElementById('allocOperatorId').value.trim();
  const counterNo = document.getElementById('allocCounterNo').value.trim();
  
  if (!operatorId || !counterNo) {
    alert('Please fill all fields');
    return;
  }
  
  showLoading('Allocating counter...');
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideLoading();
      
      if (result.success) {
        alert(`✅ Counter allocated successfully!\n\nOperator: ${operatorId}\nCounter: ${counterNo}`);
        closeCounterAllocationModal();
        
        // Reload allocations
        loadCounterAllocations();
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + result.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoading();
      alert('Error: ' + error.message);
    })
    .allocateCounter(currentUserId, operatorId, counterNo, currentUserToken);
}

/**
 * Close counter allocation modal
 */
function closeCounterAllocationModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('counterAllocationModal');
  if (modal) modal.remove();
}

/**
 * Load today's counter allocations (for supervisor)
 */
function loadCounterAllocations() {
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result.success) {
        displayCounterAllocations(result.allocations);
      }
    })
    .showTodaysAllocations(currentUserId);
}

/**
 * Display counter allocations
 */
function displayCounterAllocations(allocations) {
  let html = '<h3 style="color: #5B4B8A; margin-bottom: 15px;">Today\'s Counter Allocations</h3>';
  
  if (allocations.length === 0) {
    html += '<p style="color: #666;">No counters allocated yet today.</p>';
  } else {
    html += '<table style="width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse; font-size: 13px;">';
    html += '<thead><tr style="background: #5B4B8A; color: white;">';
    html += '<th style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Operator</th>';
    html += '<th style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Counter</th>';
    html += '<th style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">Status</th>';
    html += '</tr></thead><tbody>';
    
    allocations.forEach(alloc => {
      html += '<tr>';
      html += `<td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">${alloc.operator}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">${alloc.counterNo}</td>`;
      html += `<td style="padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #ddd;">
        <span style="background: ${alloc.status === 'OPEN' ? '#d4edda' : '#f8d7da'}; 
                     color: ${alloc.status === 'OPEN' ? '#155724' : '#721c24'}; 
                     padding: 4px 10px; border-radius: 4px; font-size: 11px;">
          ${alloc.status}
        </span>
      </td>`;
      html += '</tr>';
    });
    
    html += '</tbody></table>';
  }
  
  // Display in supervisor dashboard
  const container = document.getElementById('counterAllocationsContainer');
  if (container) {
    container.innerHTML = html;
  }
}


/**
 * Load operators into dropdown
 */
function loadOperatorsForDropdown(selectId) {
  const selectElement = document.getElementById(selectId);
  
  if (!selectElement) {
    console.error('Select element not found:', selectId);
    return;
  }
  
  // ✅ Check if currentUserId exists
  if (!currentUserId) {
    console.error('currentUserId is not set');
    selectElement.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Session expired --</option>';
    return;
  }
  
  console.log('Loading operators for dropdown:', selectId);
  selectElement.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Loading... --</option>';
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      console.log('Operators response:', result);
      
      if (result && result.success) {
        if (result.operators && result.operators.length > 0) {
          let options = '<option value="">-- Select Operator --</option>';
          result.operators.forEach(op => {
            options += `<option value="${op.operatorId}">${op.operatorId} - ${op.name}</option>`;
          });
          selectElement.innerHTML = options;
          console.log('✅ Loaded ' + result.operators.length + ' operators');
        } else {
          selectElement.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- No operators found --</option>';
          console.warn('⚠️ No operators found for branch:', result.branchCode);
        }
      } else {
        selectElement.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Error: ' + escapeHtml(result.message || 'Unknown error') + ' --</option>';
        console.error('❌ Error loading operators:', result.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      console.error('❌ Failed to load operators:', error);
      selectElement.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Error: ' + escapeHtml(error.message) + ' --</option>';
    })
    .getOperatorsForBranch(currentUserId);
}
/**
 * Show Cash Transfer Modal (Supervisor to Operator)
 */
function showCashTransferModal() {
  const html = `
    <div style="max-width: 500px; margin: 20px auto; background: white; padding: 30px; border-radius: 15px;">
      <h2 style="color: #27ae60; margin-bottom: 25px; text-align: center;">💸 Transfer Cash to Operator</h2>
      
      <div style="background: #e8f5e9; padding: 15px; border-radius: 8px; margin-bottom: 20px; border-left: 4px solid #27ae60;">
        <p style="margin: 0; color: #27ae60; font-size: 14px;">
          <strong>ℹ️ Note:</strong> Transfer cash from your wallet to operator's wallet for counter operations.
        </p>
      </div>
      
      <div class="form-group">
  <label><strong>Operator ID:</strong></label>
  <select id="transferOperatorId" style="width: 100%; padding: 12px; border: 2px solid #ddd; border-radius: 8px; margin-top: 8px; font-size: 16px;">
    <option value="">-- Loading operators... --</option>
  </select>
</div>
      <div class="form-group" style="margin-top: 20px;">
        <label><strong>Amount to Transfer:</strong></label>
        <input type="number" id="transferAmount" placeholder="Enter amount (e.g., 5000)" min="100" step="100" style="width: 100%; padding: 12px; border: 2px solid #ddd; border-radius: 8px; margin-top: 8px; font-size: 16px;">

        <label><strong>Remarks:</strong></label>
        <textarea id="transferRemarks" placeholder="Enter remarks (e.g., Counter opening cash)" rows="3" style="width: 100%; padding: 12px; border: 2px solid #ddd; border-radius: 8px; margin-top: 8px; font-size: 14px; resize: vertical;"></textarea>
      </div>
      
      <div id="transferMessage" style="margin-top: 15px; padding: 10px; border-radius: 5px; display: none;"></div>

        <button onclick="submitCashTransfer()" style="background: #27ae60; color: white; padding: 14px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold; flex: 1;">
          ✅ Transfer Cash
        </button>
        <button onclick="closeCashTransferModal()" style="background: #6c757d; color: white; padding: 14px 30px; border: none; border-radius: 8px; cursor: pointer; font-size: 16px; flex: 1;">
          Cancel
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  `;
  
  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'cashTransferModal';
  modal.style.cssText = 'position: fixed; top: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; background: rgba(0,0,0,0.8); z-index: 10000; overflow-y: auto; padding: 20px; display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;';
  modal.innerHTML = html;
  
  document.body.appendChild(modal);
  // Load operators for dropdown
loadOperatorsForDropdown('transferOperatorId');
}

/**
 * Submit Cash Transfer
 */
function submitCashTransfer() {
  const operatorId = document.getElementById('transferOperatorId').value.trim();
  const amount = document.getElementById('transferAmount').value.trim();
  const remarks = document.getElementById('transferRemarks').value.trim();
  const msgDiv = document.getElementById('transferMessage');

  // --- Validation ---
  if (!operatorId) {
    msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
    msgDiv.style.background = '#fee';
    msgDiv.style.color = '#c00';
    msgDiv.innerHTML = '❌ Please select Operator';
    return;
  }
  if (!amount || isNaN(parseFloat(amount)) || parseFloat(amount) <= 0) {
    msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
    msgDiv.style.background = '#fee';
    msgDiv.style.color = '#c00';
    msgDiv.innerHTML = '❌ Please enter a valid positive amount';
    return;
  }
  if (parseFloat(amount) < 100) {
    msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
    msgDiv.style.background = '#fee';
    msgDiv.style.color = '#c00';
    msgDiv.innerHTML = '❌ Minimum transfer amount is ₹100';
    return;
  }
  if (!remarks) {
    msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
    msgDiv.style.background = '#fff3cd';
    msgDiv.style.color = '#856404';
    msgDiv.innerHTML = '⚠️ Please enter remarks';
    return;
  }

  const amountNum = parseFloat(amount);

  // Hide old message, show loading
  msgDiv.style.display = 'none';
  showLoading('Transferring cash...');

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideLoading();

      if (result.success) {
        // ✅ FIX 1: alert() ki jagah modal use karo — GAS iFrame safe
        closeCashTransferModal();

        // ✅ FIX 2: _showSuccessModal use karo jo pehle se defined hai
        _showSuccessModal(
          '✅ Cash Transferred!',
          '💸 Operator: ' + operatorId +
          '\n📦 Amount: ₹' + amountNum.toFixed(2) +
          '\n💰 Your Balance: ₹' + (result.supervisorBalance || 0).toFixed(2) +
          (result.operatorBalance ? '\n🧾 Operator Balance: ₹' + result.operatorBalance.toFixed(2) : '') +
          '\n\n🆔 Txn ID: ' + (result.transactionId || 'N/A') +
          (result.message && result.message.includes('acknowledge') ? '\n\n⚠️ Operator must acknowledge to receive cash.' : ''),
          '#27ae60'
        );

        // ✅ FIX 3: loadSupervisorDashboard() ki jagah sahi functions call karo
        loadSupervisorDetailsNew();   // wallet refresh karta hai
        loadSupervisorOperators();    // operator wallets refresh karta hai

      } else {
        msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
        msgDiv.style.background = '#fee';
        msgDiv.style.color = '#c00';
        msgDiv.innerHTML = '❌ ' + escapeHtml(result.message);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      hideLoading();
      msgDiv.style.display = 'block';
      msgDiv.style.background = '#fee';
      msgDiv.style.color = '#c00';
      msgDiv.innerHTML = '❌ Error: ' + escapeHtml(error.message);
    })
    .transferCashToOperator(currentUserId, operatorId, amountNum, remarks, currentUserToken);
}
/**
 * Close Cash Transfer Modal
 */
function closeCashTransferModal() {
  const modal = document.getElementById('cashTransferModal');
  if (modal) modal.remove();
}
/**
 * Load Operator Wallets for Supervisor Dashboard
 */
function loadOperatorWallets() {
  const listDiv = document.getElementById('operatorsWalletList');
  
  if (!listDiv) return; // Not on supervisor dashboard
  
  listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color: white; text-align: center;">Loading operator wallets...</p>';
  
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result.success) {
        displayOperatorWallets(result.operators);
      } else {
        listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #ffcccc;">Failed to load operators</p>';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
      listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color: #ffcccc;">Error: ' + escapeHtml(error.message) + '</p>';
    })
    .getOperatorWallets(currentUserId);
}

/**
 * Display Operator Wallets
 */
function displayOperatorWallets(operators) {
  const listDiv = document.getElementById('operatorsWalletList');
  
  if (operators.length === 0) {
    listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color: rgba(255,255,255,0.7);">No operators found in your branch</p>';
    return;
  }
  
  let html = '<div style="display: grid; gap: 15px;">';
  
  operators.forEach(op => {
    const balanceColor = op.balance > 0 ? '#27ae60' : '#95a5a6';
    
    html += `
      <div style="background: white; padding: 15px; border-radius: 10px; display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr auto; gap: 15px; align-items: center;">
        <div>
          <div style="font-weight: bold; color: #2c3e50; font-size: 16px;">${op.operatorId}</div>
          <div style="font-size: 13px; color: #7f8c8d; margin-top: 3px;">${op.name || 'Operator'}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="text-align: right;">
          <div style="font-size: 11px; color: #7f8c8d;">Wallet Balance</div>
          <div style="font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; color: ${balanceColor};">₹${op.balance.toFixed(2)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  });
  
  html += '</div>';
  listDiv.innerHTML = html;
}
// ============================================
// 🛠️ UTILITY FUNCTIONS
// ============================================

/**
 * Show loading indicator
 */
function showLoading(message) {
  const existing = document.getElementById('loadingIndicator');
  if (existing) existing.remove();
  
  const loader = document.createElement('div');
  loader.id = 'loadingIndicator';
  loader.style.cssText = 'position: fixed; top: 50%; left: 50%; transform: translate(-50%, -50%); background: rgba(0,0,0,0.9); color: white; padding: 30px 40px; border-radius: 15px; z-index: 99999; text-align: center; box-shadow: 0 10px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.5);';
  loader.innerHTML = `
    <div style="font-size: 40px; margin-bottom: 15px;">⏳</div>
    <div style="font-size: 16px; font-weight: bold;">${message || 'Loading...'}</div>
  `;
  
  document.body.appendChild(loader);
}

/**
 * Hide loading indicator
 */
function hideLoading() {
  const loader = document.getElementById('loadingIndicator');
  if (loader) loader.remove();
}
