function showOfficeAcknowledgeModal() {
  const old = document.getElementById('officeAckModal');
  if (old) old.remove();

  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'officeAckModal';
  modal.style.cssText =
    'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.7);' +
    'z-index:9999;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;overflow-y:auto;padding:20px;';

  modal.innerHTML =
    '<div style="background:white;border-radius:16px;padding:30px;max-width:600px;width:100%;max-height:90vh;overflow-y:auto;">' +
      '<h2 style="color:#8e44ad;margin:0 0 10px 0;text-align:center;">🏦 Cash from Office</h2>' +
      '<p style="color:#7f8c8d;text-align:center;margin-bottom:20px;font-size:14px;">' +
        'Cash Office ne dispatch kiya — acknowledge karo aur wallet mein add karo' +
      '</p>' +
      '<div id="officeAckList">' +
        '<div style="text-align:center;padding:20px;">' +
          '<div class="spinner" style="margin:0 auto;"></div>' +
          '<p style="color:#7f8c8d;margin-top:10px;">Loading...</p>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="margin-top:20px;text-align:center;">' +
        '<button onclick="document.getElementById(\'officeAckModal\').remove()" ' +
          'style="background:#6c757d;color:white;padding:12px 30px;border:none;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:16px;">Close</button>' +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>';

  document.body.appendChild(modal);
  _loadOfficePendingTxns();
}

function _loadOfficePendingTxns() {
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      const listDiv = document.getElementById('officeAckList');
      if (!listDiv) return;

      if (!result || !result.success || !result.transactions || result.transactions.length === 0) {
        listDiv.innerHTML =
          '<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px 20px;">' +
            '<div style="font-size:64px;margin-bottom:15px;">✅</div>' +
            '<p style="color:#7f8c8d;font-size:16px;">No pending office transfers</p>' +
          '</div>';

        const badge = document.getElementById('officeAckBadge');
        if (badge) badge.style.display = 'none';
        return;
      }

      // Update badge
      const badge = document.getElementById('officeAckBadge');
      if (badge) {
        badge.textContent = result.transactions.length;
        badge.style.display = 'inline-block';
      }

      var html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:15px;">';
result.transactions.forEach(function(t) {
  // ✅ FIX: Variables pehle calculate karo — template mein complex expression nahi
  var amt       = parseFloat(t.amount) || 0;
  var amtDisplay = '₹' + amt.toLocaleString('en-IN', {minimumFractionDigits: 2});
  var txnId     = (t.txnId   || '').replace(/'/g, "\\'");   // quote escape
  var officeId  = (t.officeId || '').replace(/'/g, "\\'");

  html +=
    '<div style="background:#f0e6ff;padding:20px;border-radius:10px;border-left:4px solid #8e44ad;">' +

      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:start;margin-bottom:15px;">' +
        '<div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#6c3483;font-weight:bold;">FROM OFFICE</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:16px;color:#2c3e50;font-weight:bold;">🏦 ' + (t.officeId || '') + '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div style="text-align:right;">' +
          '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#6c3483;font-weight:bold;">AMOUNT</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:28px;color:#8e44ad;font-weight:bold;">' + amtDisplay + '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px;margin-bottom:15px;">' +
        '<div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#6c3483;">TXN ID</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:13px;color:#2c3e50;font-weight:600;font-family:monospace;">' + (t.txnId || '') + '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#6c3483;">DATE</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:13px;color:#2c3e50;">' + (t.date || '') + '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>' +

      (t.remarks ? '<div style="font-size:12px;color:#7f8c8d;margin-bottom:10px;">📝 ' + t.remarks + '</div>' : '') +

      // ✅ FIX: Button text seedha string — koi ternary nahi
      '<button onclick="_confirmOfficeAck(\'' + txnId + '\', ' + amt + ', \'' + officeId + '\')" ' +
        'style="width:100%;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#8e44ad,#9b59b6);color:white;padding:12px;' +
        'border:none;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:15px;font-weight:bold;">' +
        '✅ Acknowledge & Add ' + amtDisplay + ' to Wallet' +
      '</button>' +

    '</div>';
});
html += '</div>';
listDiv.innerHTML = html;
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      const listDiv = document.getElementById('officeAckList');
      if (listDiv) listDiv.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#e74c3c;text-align:center;">❌ Error: ' + escapeHtml(err.message) + '</p>';
    })
    .getPendingOfficeTobranchTxns(currentUserId);
}

function _confirmOfficeAck(txnId, amount, officeId) {
  if (!confirm('Acknowledge ₹' + amount + ' received from Cash Office ' + officeId + '?\n\nYeh amount aapke wallet mein add hoga.')) return;

  const modal   = document.getElementById('officeAckModal');
  const listDiv = document.getElementById('officeAckList');
  if (listDiv) {
    listDiv.innerHTML =
      '<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;">' +
        '<div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:15px;">⏳</div>' +
        '<p style="font-weight:bold;color:#2c3e50;">Acknowledging...</p>' +
      '</div>';
  }

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (modal) modal.remove();
      if (result && result.success) {
        _showSuccessModal(
          '✅ Cash Acknowledged!',
          (result.message || '✅ Cash from Office acknowledged!\n\nAmount: ₹' + amount + '\nNew Balance: ₹' + (result.newBalance || 0)),
          '#8e44ad'
        );
        if (typeof startSupervisorLiveRefresh === 'function') startSupervisorLiveRefresh();
        loadSupervisorOfficeAckCount();
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + (result ? result.message : 'Error'));
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      if (modal) modal.remove();
      alert('❌ Error: ' + err.message);
    })
    .supervisorAcknowledgeCashFromOffice(currentUserId, txnId);
}

// ================================================================
// SUPERVISOR: Send Cash to Office
// ================================================================
function showSendToOfficeModal() {
  const old = document.getElementById('sendToOfficeModal');
  if (old) old.remove();

  const modal = document.createElement('div');
  modal.id = 'sendToOfficeModal';
  modal.style.cssText =
    'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.7);' +
    'z-index:9999;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;padding:20px;';

  const walletEl  = document.getElementById('supWalletDisplay');
  const curBal    = walletEl ? (parseFloat(walletEl.textContent.replace('₹','').replace(',','')) || 0) : 0;

  modal.innerHTML =
    '<div style="background:white;border-radius:16px;padding:30px;max-width:420px;width:100%;max-height:90vh;overflow-y:auto;">' +
      '<h3 style="text-align:center;color:#2c3e50;margin:0 0 20px 0;">🏦 Send Cash to Office</h3>' +

      '<div style="background:#f8f9fa;border-radius:10px;padding:15px;margin-bottom:20px;text-align:center;">' +
        '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#7f8c8d;font-weight:bold;margin-bottom:5px;">YOUR WALLET</div>' +
        '<div style="font-size:28px;font-weight:bold;color:#f39c12;">₹' + curBal.toFixed(2) + '</div>' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div style="margin-bottom:15px;">' +
        '<label style="display:block;font-size:13px;font-weight:bold;color:#2c3e50;margin-bottom:8px;">Cash Office</label>' +
        '<select id="sendOfficeSelect" style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:2px solid #e0e0e0;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;">' +
          '<option value="">Loading offices...</option>' +
        '</select>' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div style="margin-bottom:15px;">' +
        '<label style="display:block;font-size:13px;font-weight:bold;color:#2c3e50;margin-bottom:8px;">Amount (₹)</label>' +
        '<input type="number" id="sendOfficeAmount" placeholder="0.00" ' +
          'style="width:100%;padding:12px;border:2px solid #e0e0e0;border-radius:8px;font-size:16px;box-sizing:border-box;" ' +
          'min="0" max="' + curBal + '" step="0.01">' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div style="margin-bottom:20px;">' +
        '<label style="display:block;font-size:13px;font-weight:bold;color:#2c3e50;margin-bottom:8px;">Remarks (optional)</label>' +
        '<input type="text" id="sendOfficeRemarks" placeholder="e.g. Excess cash deposit" ' +
          'style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:2px solid #e0e0e0;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;box-sizing:border-box;">' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div style="background:#e3f2fd;border-radius:8px;padding:12px;margin-bottom:20px;">' +
        '<p style="margin:0;color:#1976d2;font-size:12px;line-height:1.5;">' +
          'ℹ️ Cash turant aapke wallet se deduct hoga.<br>' +
          'Cash Office (Treasurer) acknowledge karega.' +
        '</p>' +
      '</div>' +

      '<div style="display:flex;gap:10px;">' +
        '<button onclick="document.getElementById(\'sendToOfficeModal\').remove()" ' +
          'style="flex:1;padding:12px;background:#ecf0f1;border:none;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;">Cancel</button>' +
        '<button onclick="_confirmSendToOffice(' + curBal + ')" ' +
          'style="flex:1;padding:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#2980b9,#3498db);border:none;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;color:white;">🏦 Send</button>' +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>';

  document.body.appendChild(modal);

  // Load offices into dropdown
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      const sel = document.getElementById('sendOfficeSelect');
      if (!sel) return;
      sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select Office --</option>';
      if (res && res.success && res.offices) {
        res.offices.forEach(function(o) {
          sel.innerHTML += '<option value="' + o.officeId + '">' + o.officeId + ' — ' + (o.officeName || '') + '</option>';
        });
      }
      if (!res || !res.offices || res.offices.length === 0) {
        const msg = (res && res.message) ? res.message : 'Aapki branch kisi Cash Office se mapped nahi hai.';
        sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">⚠️ ' + msg + '</option>';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function() {
      const sel = document.getElementById('sendOfficeSelect');
      if (sel) sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Error loading offices</option>';
    })
    .getMappedCashOfficesForSupervisor(currentUserId);
}

function _confirmSendToOffice(maxBal) {
  const officeId = document.getElementById('sendOfficeSelect').value;
  const amount   = parseFloat(document.getElementById('sendOfficeAmount').value);
  const remarks  = document.getElementById('sendOfficeRemarks').value.trim();

  if (!officeId) { alert('⚠️ Office select karo!'); return; }
  if (!amount || amount <= 0) { alert('⚠️ Valid amount enter karo!'); return; }
  if (amount > maxBal) { alert('⚠️ Wallet balance insufficient!\n\nAvailable: ₹' + maxBal.toFixed(2)); return; }

  const modal = document.getElementById('sendToOfficeModal');
  if (modal) {
    modal.innerHTML =
      '<div style="background:white;border-radius:16px;padding:40px;max-width:340px;width:90%;text-align:center;">' +
        '<div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:15px;">⏳</div>' +
        '<p style="font-weight:bold;color:#2c3e50;">Sending ₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + ' to office...</p>' +
      '</div>';
  }

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (modal) modal.remove();
      if (result && result.success) {
        _showSuccessModal(
          '✅ Cash Sent to Office!',
          result.message || ('₹' + amount.toFixed(2) + ' sent to office ' + officeId + '.\n\nTreasurer will acknowledge.'),
          '#2980b9'
        );
        if (typeof startSupervisorLiveRefresh === 'function') startSupervisorLiveRefresh();
      } else {
        alert('❌ ' + (result ? result.message : 'Error'));
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      if (modal) modal.remove();
      alert('❌ Error: ' + err.message);
    })
    .supervisorSendCashToOffice(currentUserId, officeId, amount, remarks, currentUserToken);
}

// Load office acknowledgement count for badge
function loadSupervisorOfficeAckCount() {
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      const badge = document.getElementById('officeAckBadge');
      if (!badge) return;
      if (result && result.success && result.count > 0) {
        badge.textContent = result.count;
        badge.style.display = 'inline-block';
      } else {
        badge.style.display = 'none';
      }
    })
    .getPendingOfficeTobranchTxns(currentUserId);
}

function startSupervisorLiveRefresh() {
  if (window._supervisorRefreshInterval) {
    clearInterval(window._supervisorRefreshInterval);
  }

  _doSupervisorLiveRefresh();
  window._supervisorRefreshInterval = setInterval(_doSupervisorLiveRefresh, 30000);
}

function _doSupervisorLiveRefresh() {
  if (!currentUserId || currentUserRole !== 'SUPERVISOR') return;

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (!result || !result.success) return;

      const supWalletEl = document.getElementById('supWalletDisplay');
      if (supWalletEl) {
        const newBal = parseFloat(result.balance) || 0;
        supWalletEl.textContent = '₹' + newBal.toFixed(2);
        _pulseElement('supWalletDisplay');
      }

      const opWalletList = document.getElementById('operatorsWalletList');
      if (opWalletList && result.operators && result.operators.length > 0) {
        let html = '';
        result.operators.forEach(function(op) {
          const balColor = op.balance > 0 ? '#e74c3c' : '#27ae60';
          const balIcon  = op.balance > 0 ? '💰' : '✅';
          html += '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;' +
                  'padding:10px 15px;border-bottom:1px solid #f0f0f0;">' +
                  '<span style="font-weight:600;color:#2c3e50;">👤 ' + op.operatorId + '</span>' +
                  '<span style="font-size:16px;font-weight:bold;color:' + balColor + ';">' +
                  balIcon + ' ₹' + (parseFloat(op.balance)||0).toFixed(2) + '</span>' +
                  '</div>';
        });
        opWalletList.innerHTML = html;
      }

      const openCountBadge = document.getElementById('openCountersBadge');
      if (openCountBadge) {
        openCountBadge.textContent = result.openCounterCount || 0;
        openCountBadge.style.display = result.openCounterCount > 0 ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
      }

      const pendingBadge = document.getElementById('pendingCountBadge');
      if (pendingBadge) {
        pendingBadge.textContent = result.pendingCount || 0;
      }

      // ── NEW: Cash return count badge ──────────────────────────
      const returnBadge = document.getElementById('returnCountBadge');
      if (returnBadge) {
        if (result.returnCount > 0) {
          returnBadge.textContent = result.returnCount;
          returnBadge.style.display = 'inline-block';
        } else {
          returnBadge.style.display = 'none';
        }
      }

      _updateRefreshTimestamp('supLastRefresh');

      // ── Current Day card ─────────────────────────────────────
      const supDayEl  = document.getElementById('supActiveDayDisplay');
      const supLblEl  = document.getElementById('supActiveDayLabel');
      if (supDayEl) {
       supDayEl.textContent = result.activeDayDateDisplay || '—';
// ✅ FIX: Day date sessionStorage mein save karo Other Entry ke liye
if (result.activeDayDate) {
    sessionStorage.setItem('activeDayDate', result.activeDayDate);
} // ← ADD
        if (supLblEl) {
          if (!result.activeDayDateDisplay) {
            supLblEl.textContent = '⛔ Day not started';
          } else if (result.dayStarted) {
            supLblEl.textContent = '✅ Day Open';
            supLblEl.style.color = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.7)';
          } else {
            supLblEl.textContent = '⚠️ Yeh din band nahi hua!';
            supLblEl.style.color = '#ffeb3b';
          }
        }
      }

      // ── FIX: Previous day restriction — disable supervisor menu ─
      if (result.isPreviousDay || result.mustCloseFirst) {
        setSupervisorPreviousDayMode(result.openDayDate || result.activeDayDateDisplay);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      console.warn('Supervisor live refresh failed:', err);
    })
    .getSupervisorLiveDashboard(currentUserId);
}

function stopSupervisorLiveRefresh() {
  if (window._supervisorRefreshInterval) {
    clearInterval(window._supervisorRefreshInterval);
    window._supervisorRefreshInterval = null;
  }
}

// Backward compatibility alias
function startWalletAutoRefresh() {
  if (currentUserRole === 'OPERATOR')   startOperatorLiveRefresh();
  if (currentUserRole === 'SUPERVISOR') startSupervisorLiveRefresh();
}
function stopWalletAutoRefresh() {
  stopOperatorLiveRefresh();
  stopSupervisorLiveRefresh();
}

// ✅ FIX 3: Toast notification for operator form state changes
function _showOpToast(msg) {
  var old = document.getElementById('_opToastBanner');
  if (old) old.remove();
  var t = document.createElement('div');
  t.id = '_opToastBanner';
  t.style.cssText =
    'position:fixed;top:18px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);' +
    'background:linear-gradient(135deg,#27ae60,#2ecc71);color:#fff;' +
    'padding:12px 22px;border-radius:12px;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;' +
    'z-index:99999;box-shadow:0 6px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.25);' +
    'animation:_toastSlide 0.35s ease;max-width:88vw;text-align:center;';
  t.textContent = msg;
  document.body.appendChild(t);
  setTimeout(function() {
    t.style.transition = 'opacity 0.45s';
    t.style.opacity = '0';
    setTimeout(function() { if (t.parentNode) t.remove(); }, 450);
  }, 4000);
}

function _pulseElement(id) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (!el) return;
  el.style.transition = 'transform 0.2s ease, opacity 0.2s ease';
  el.style.transform = 'scale(1.12)';
  el.style.opacity   = '0.8';
  setTimeout(function() {
    el.style.transform = 'scale(1)';
    el.style.opacity   = '1';
  }, 300);
}

function _updateRefreshTimestamp(elementId) {
  const el = document.getElementById(elementId);
  if (!el) return;
  const now = new Date();
  el.textContent = 'Updated: ' +
    now.getHours().toString().padStart(2,'0') + ':' +
    now.getMinutes().toString().padStart(2,'0') + ':' +
    now.getSeconds().toString().padStart(2,'0');
}
// ============================================
// DAILY ACCOUNT REPORT — FRESH SYSTEM
// ============================================
function showDailyReportSection() {
  showSection('dailyReportSection');
  var today = new Date();
  var el = document.getElementById('dailyReportDate');
  if (el) el.value = today.getFullYear() + '-' +
    String(today.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0') + '-' +
    String(today.getDate()).padStart(2,'0');
}

function loadDailyReport(dateValue) {
  var reportDateStr = '';
  if (dateValue && String(dateValue).trim()) {
    var parts = String(dateValue).split('-');
    if (parts.length === 3) {
      reportDateStr = parts[2] + '/' + parts[1] + '/' + parts[0];
    }
  }
  var container = document.getElementById('dailyReportContent');
  container.innerHTML =
    '<div style="text-align:center;padding:50px;">' +
      '<div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:12px;">⏳</div>' +
      '<p style="color:white;font-size:15px;">Report generate ho raha hai...</p>' +
    '</div>';

  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (result && result.success) {
        renderDailyReport(result);
      } else {
        container.innerHTML =
          '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#ff6b6b;font-size:15px;">❌ ' +
          (result ? result.message : 'Unknown error') + '</div>';
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      container.innerHTML =
        '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#ff6b6b;font-size:15px;">❌ ' + err.message + '</div>';
    })
    .getBranchDailyReport(currentUserId, reportDateStr);
}

function renderDailyReport(data) {
  var fmt = function(n) {
    return '₹' + (parseFloat(n)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN', { minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2 });
  };

  var statusBadge = '';
  if (data.dayStatus === 'OPEN') {
    statusBadge = '<span style="background:#f39c12;color:#fff;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:12px;font-size:11px;font-weight:bold;margin-left:8px;">🟡 DAY OPEN</span>';
  } else if (data.dayStatus === 'CLOSED') {
    statusBadge = '<span style="background:#27ae60;color:#fff;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:12px;font-size:11px;font-weight:bold;margin-left:8px;">🟢 DAY CLOSED</span>';
  } else {
    statusBadge = '<span style="background:#95a5a6;color:#fff;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:12px;font-size:11px;font-weight:bold;margin-left:8px;">⚪ NO LOG</span>';
  }

  var balNote = '';
  if (data.balanceSource === 'SAVED') {
    balNote = '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#27ae60;margin-top:3px;">✅ Saved snapshot (accurate)</div>';
  } else if (data.balanceSource === 'LIVE') {
    balNote = '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#f39c12;margin-top:3px;">🔄 Live (day still open)</div>';
  } else {
    balNote = '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#e74c3c;margin-top:3px;">⚠️ Computed — Day Start/End karo to save ho</div>';
  }

  var html =
    '<div id="dailyReportPrintArea" style="background:#fff;border-radius:12px;overflow:hidden;color:#2c3e50;">' +

    '<div style="background:linear-gradient(135deg,#1a237e,#283593);color:white;padding:18px 20px;">' +
      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:8px;">' +
        '<div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:11px;opacity:0.75;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;">Daily Account Report</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:bold;margin-top:2px;">Branch: ' + data.branchCode + statusBadge + '</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:13px;opacity:0.85;margin-top:4px;">📅 ' + data.reportDate + '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;" class="no-print">' +
          '<button onclick="printDailyReport()" style="background:rgba(255,255,255,0.2);color:white;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.4);padding:8px 16px;border-radius:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:13px;font-weight:bold;">🖨️ Print</button>' +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>' +

    '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:0;border-bottom:2px solid #e0e0e0;">' +
      '<div style="padding:14px 18px;background:#f8f9ff;border-right:1px solid #e0e0e0;">' +
        '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#666;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Opening Balance</div>' +
        '<div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:bold;color:#1a237e;margin-top:4px;">' + fmt(data.openingBalance) + '</div>' +
        '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#888;margin-top:2px;">Day begin ka balance</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="padding:14px 18px;background:#f0fff4;">' +
        '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#666;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.5px;">Closing Balance</div>' +
        '<div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:bold;color:#27ae60;margin-top:4px;">' + fmt(data.closingBalance) + '</div>' +
        balNote +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>' +

    '<div id="rptPanelTotal" style="display:block;padding:18px;">' + _totalReportHTML(data, fmt) + '</div>' +

    '</div>';

  document.getElementById('dailyReportContent').innerHTML = html;
}

function switchRptTab(activeTabId, activePanelId) {
  // Only Total Report tab exists now — Scheme/Operator moved to Reports Menu
  var t = document.getElementById('rptTabTotal');
  if (t) {
    t.style.background   = '#fff';
    t.style.color        = '#1a237e';
    t.style.borderBottom = '3px solid #1a237e';
  }
  var p = document.getElementById('rptPanelTotal');
  if (p) p.style.display = 'block';
}

// ── TOTAL REPORT ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
function _totalReportHTML(data, fmt) {
  var r = data.receipts;
  var p = data.payments;

  function sRow(label, amount, color, bold) {
    var fw = bold ? '700' : '500';
    var bg = bold ? '#f0f4ff' : 'transparent';
    return '<tr style="background:' + bg + ';">' +
      '<td style="padding:9px 12px;font-weight:' + fw + ';color:#333;font-size:13px;">' + label + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:9px 12px;text-align:right;font-weight:' + fw + ';color:' + color + ';font-size:13px;">' + fmt(amount) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }

  function dRows(details) {
    if (!details || !details.length) return '';
    var rows = '';
    details.slice(0,8).forEach(function(d) {
      var line = [];
      if (d.accountNo || d.loanAcNo) line.push('<b>' + (d.accountNo||d.loanAcNo) + '</b>');
      if (d.name) line.push(d.name);
      if (d.amount !== undefined) line.push('₹' + (parseFloat(d.amount)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN'));
      if (d.interest) line.push('+Int ₹' + (parseFloat(d.interest)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN'));
      if (d.fee) line.push('+Fee ₹' + (parseFloat(d.fee)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN'));
      if (d.monthFor) line.push(d.monthFor);
      if (d.scheme) line.push('<span style="background:#e3f2fd;color:#1565c0;padding:1px 5px;border-radius:3px;font-size:10px;">' + d.scheme + '</span>');
      rows += '<tr style="background:#fafafa;"><td colspan="2" style="padding:4px 12px 4px 24px;font-size:11px;color:#666;border-bottom:1px dotted #e0e0e0;">' + line.join(' &nbsp;|&nbsp; ') + '</td></tr>';
    });
    if (details.length > 8) rows += '<tr style="background:#fafafa;"><td colspan="2" style="padding:3px 12px 3px 24px;font-size:11px;color:#999;font-style:italic;">...aur ' + (details.length-8) + ' entries</td></tr>';
    return rows;
  }

  var net = r.grandTotal - p.grandTotal;
  return '<div style="overflow-x:auto;">' +
  '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">' +
  '<tr><th colspan="2" style="background:#e8f5e9;color:#2e7d32;padding:10px 12px;text-align:left;font-size:13px;">📥 RECEIPTS</th></tr>' +
  sRow('Deposit Collections', r.deposits.total, '#2e7d32') + dRows(r.deposits.details) +
  sRow('Loan Repayments', r.repayments.total, '#2e7d32') + dRows(r.repayments.details) +
  sRow('Cash from Cash Office', r.cashFromOffice.total, '#2e7d32') + dRows(r.cashFromOffice.details) +
  sRow('Other Receipts', r.other.total, '#2e7d32') + dRows(r.other.details) +
  sRow('TOTAL RECEIPTS', r.grandTotal, '#2e7d32', true) +
  '<tr><th colspan="2" style="background:#fce4ec;color:#c62828;padding:10px 12px;text-align:left;font-size:13px;border-top:8px solid #f5f5f5;">📤 PAYMENTS</th></tr>' +
  sRow('Loan Disbursements', p.loanDisburse.total, '#c62828') + dRows(p.loanDisburse.details) +
  sRow('Account Close Settlements', p.settlements.total, '#c62828') + dRows(p.settlements.details) +
  sRow('Cash to Cash Office', p.cashToOffice.total, '#c62828') + dRows(p.cashToOffice.details) +
  sRow('Other Payments', p.other.total, '#c62828') + dRows(p.other.details) +
  sRow('TOTAL PAYMENTS', p.grandTotal, '#c62828', true) +
  '<tr style="background:#fff8e1;"><td style="padding:10px 12px;font-weight:700;font-size:13px;color:#e65100;">NET CASH FLOW</td>' +
  '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-weight:700;font-size:14px;color:' + (net>=0?'#2e7d32':'#c62828') + ';">' + fmt(net) + '</td></tr>' +
  '</table></div>' +
  '<div style="margin-top:16px;border:2px solid #1a237e;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">' +
    '<div style="background:#1a237e;color:white;padding:10px 14px;font-weight:bold;font-size:13px;">🔢 Balance Reconciliation</div>' +
    '<div style="padding:12px 14px;background:#f8f9ff;">' +
      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px dashed #e0e0e0;font-size:13px;"><span style="color:#555;">Opening Balance</span><span style="font-weight:600;">' + fmt(data.openingBalance) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px dashed #e0e0e0;font-size:13px;"><span style="color:#2e7d32;">+ Total Receipts</span><span style="color:#2e7d32;font-weight:600;">' + fmt(r.grandTotal) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px dashed #e0e0e0;font-size:13px;"><span style="color:#c62828;">− Total Payments</span><span style="color:#c62828;font-weight:600;">' + fmt(p.grandTotal) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:8px 0;font-size:15px;font-weight:bold;"><span style="color:#1a237e;">= Closing Balance</span><span style="color:#27ae60;">' + fmt(data.closingBalance) + '</span></div>' +
    '</div>' +
  '</div>';
}

// ── SCHEME-WISE REPORT ────────────────────────────────────────────
function _schemeReportHTML(data, fmt) {
  var schemes = data.schemeSummary;
  if (!schemes || !schemes.length) {
    return '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#999;">Koi scheme data nahi mila is date ke liye.</div>';
  }
  var rows = '';
  var tIn = 0, tOut = 0;
  schemes.forEach(function(s) {
    tIn  += s.totalIn;
    tOut += s.totalOut;
    var net = s.totalIn - s.totalOut;
    rows += '<tr style="border-bottom:1px solid #e0e0e0;">' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;font-weight:600;color:#1a237e;font-size:13px;">' + s.scheme + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(s.deposits) + (s.depCount ? '<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:#888;">' + s.depCount + ' txn</span>' : '') + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(s.repayments) + (s.repCount ? '<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:#888;">' + s.repCount + ' txn</span>' : '') + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-weight:700;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(s.totalIn) + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#c62828;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(s.disburse) + (s.disCount ? '<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:#888;">' + s.disCount + ' txn</span>' : '') + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-weight:700;color:' + (net>=0?'#2e7d32':'#c62828') + ';font-size:13px;">' + fmt(net) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  });
  var html = '<div style="overflow-x:auto;">' +
  '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">' +
  '<thead><tr style="background:#e8eaf6;">' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:left;font-size:12px;color:#1a237e;">Scheme / Type</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#2e7d32;">Deposits</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#2e7d32;">Repayments</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#2e7d32;">Total IN</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#c62828;">Disburse</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#333;">Net</th>' +
  '</tr></thead><tbody>' + rows + '</tbody>' +
  '<tfoot><tr style="background:#e8eaf6;font-weight:bold;">' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;font-size:13px;">TOTAL</td>' +
    '<td colspan="2"></td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(tIn) + '</td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#c62828;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(tOut) + '</td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:13px;color:' + (tIn-tOut>=0?'#2e7d32':'#c62828') + ';">' + fmt(tIn-tOut) + '</td>' +
  '</tr></tfoot></table></div>';

  // Scheme detail cards
  if (data.depositByScheme && Object.keys(data.depositByScheme).length) {
    html += '<div style="margin-top:18px;"><div style="font-weight:bold;color:#333;margin-bottom:10px;font-size:14px;">📦 Scheme-wise Deposit Details</div><div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(260px,1fr));gap:10px;">';
    Object.keys(data.depositByScheme).forEach(function(sch) {
      var sd = data.depositByScheme[sch];
      html += '<div style="border:1px solid #c5cae9;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">' +
        '<div style="background:#e8eaf6;padding:8px 12px;font-weight:bold;font-size:12px;color:#1a237e;">' + sch + ' (' + sd.count + ' txn) — ' + fmt(sd.total) + '</div>' +
        '<div style="padding:8px 12px;">';
      sd.details.slice(0,6).forEach(function(d) {
        html += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#666;padding:2px 0;border-bottom:1px dotted #e0e0e0;">' +
          (d.accountNo||'') + ' · ' + (d.name||'') + ' · ₹' + (parseFloat(d.amount)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN') + '</div>';
      });
      if (sd.details.length > 6) html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#999;">+' + (sd.details.length-6) + ' more</div>';
      html += '</div></div>';
    });
    html += '</div></div>';
  }

  if (data.disburseByScheme && Object.keys(data.disburseByScheme).length) {
    html += '<div style="margin-top:14px;"><div style="font-weight:bold;color:#c62828;margin-bottom:10px;font-size:14px;">💸 Scheme-wise Disbursement Details</div><div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(260px,1fr));gap:10px;">';
    Object.keys(data.disburseByScheme).forEach(function(sch) {
      var sd = data.disburseByScheme[sch];
      html += '<div style="border:1px solid #ffcdd2;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;">' +
        '<div style="background:#fce4ec;padding:8px 12px;font-weight:bold;font-size:12px;color:#c62828;">' + sch + ' (' + sd.count + ' txn) — ' + fmt(sd.total) + '</div>' +
        '<div style="padding:8px 12px;">';
      sd.details.slice(0,6).forEach(function(d) {
        html += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#666;padding:2px 0;border-bottom:1px dotted #e0e0e0;">' +
          (d.loanAcNo||'') + ' · ' + (d.name||'') + ' · ₹' + (parseFloat(d.amount)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN') + '</div>';
      });
      if (sd.details.length > 6) html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#999;">+' + (sd.details.length-6) + ' more</div>';
      html += '</div></div>';
    });
    html += '</div></div>';
  }
  return html;
}

// ── OPERATOR-WISE REPORT ──────────────────────────────────────────
function _operatorReportHTML(data, fmt) {
  var ops = data.operatorSummary;
  if (!ops || !ops.length) {
    return '<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:#999;">Koi operator data nahi mila is date ke liye.</div>';
  }
  var rows = '';
  var tDep=0, tRep=0, tDis=0, tSet=0, tIn=0, tOut=0;
  ops.forEach(function(op) {
    tDep+=op.deposits; tRep+=op.repayments;
    tDis+=op.disburse; tSet+=op.settlements;
    tIn+=op.totalIn;   tOut+=op.totalOut;
    rows += '<tr style="border-bottom:1px solid #e0e0e0;">' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;font-weight:600;font-size:13px;color:#333;">' + op.operatorId + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(op.deposits) + (op.depCount ? '<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:#888;">' + op.depCount + ' txn</span>' : '') + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(op.repayments) + (op.repCount ? '<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:#888;">' + op.repCount + ' txn</span>' : '') + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-weight:700;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(op.totalIn) + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#c62828;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(op.disburse) + (op.disCount ? '<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:#888;">' + op.disCount + ' txn</span>' : '') + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#c62828;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(op.settlements) + (op.setCount ? '<br><span style="font-size:10px;color:#888;">' + op.setCount + ' txn</span>' : '') + '</td>' +
      '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-weight:700;font-size:13px;color:' + (op.net>=0?'#2e7d32':'#c62828') + ';">' + fmt(op.net) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  });
  var html = '<div style="overflow-x:auto;">' +
  '<table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-family:Arial,sans-serif;">' +
  '<thead><tr style="background:#fce4ec;">' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:left;font-size:12px;color:#880e4f;">Operator ID</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#2e7d32;">Deposits</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#2e7d32;">Repayments</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#2e7d32;">Total IN</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#c62828;">Disburse</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#c62828;">Settlements</th>' +
    '<th style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#333;">Net</th>' +
  '</tr></thead><tbody>' + rows + '</tbody>' +
  '<tfoot><tr style="background:#fce4ec;font-weight:bold;">' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;font-size:13px;">TOTAL</td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(tDep) + '</td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(tRep) + '</td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#2e7d32;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(tIn) + '</td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#c62828;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(tDis) + '</td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;color:#c62828;font-size:13px;">' + fmt(tSet) + '</td>' +
    '<td style="padding:10px 12px;text-align:right;font-size:13px;color:' + (tIn-tOut>=0?'#2e7d32':'#c62828') + ';">' + fmt(tIn-tOut) + '</td>' +
  '</tr></tfoot></table></div>';

  // Operator detail cards
  html += '<div style="margin-top:18px;"><div style="font-weight:bold;color:#333;margin-bottom:10px;font-size:14px;">📋 Operator Detail Cards</div>' +
    '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(280px,1fr));gap:12px;">';
  ops.forEach(function(op) {
    var depDets = (data.depositByOperator[op.operatorId]  || {}).details || [];
    var repDets = (data.repayByOperator[op.operatorId]    || {}).details || [];
    var disDets = (data.disburseByOperator[op.operatorId] || {}).details || [];
    html += '<div style="border:1px solid #e0e0e0;border-radius:10px;overflow:hidden;">' +
      '<div style="background:#37474f;color:white;padding:10px 14px;font-weight:bold;font-size:13px;">👤 ' + op.operatorId + '</div>' +
      '<div style="padding:12px 14px;">' +
        '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:6px;margin-bottom:10px;">' +
          '<div style="background:#e8f5e9;border-radius:6px;padding:6px 8px;text-align:center;"><div style="font-size:10px;color:#666;">Deposits</div><div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:#2e7d32;">' + fmt(op.deposits) + '</div></div>' +
          '<div style="background:#e8f5e9;border-radius:6px;padding:6px 8px;text-align:center;"><div style="font-size:10px;color:#666;">Repayments</div><div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:#2e7d32;">' + fmt(op.repayments) + '</div></div>' +
          '<div style="background:#fce4ec;border-radius:6px;padding:6px 8px;text-align:center;"><div style="font-size:10px;color:#666;">Disburse</div><div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:#c62828;">' + fmt(op.disburse) + '</div></div>' +
        '</div>';
    if (depDets.length) {
      html += '<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:#333;margin-bottom:3px;">Deposits</div>';
      depDets.slice(0,4).forEach(function(d) {
        html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#666;padding:2px 0;border-bottom:1px dotted #eee;">' +
          (d.accountNo||'') + ' · ' + (d.name||'').substring(0,18) + ' · ₹' + (parseFloat(d.amount)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN') +
          (d.scheme ? ' <span style="background:#e3f2fd;padding:0 4px;border-radius:3px;">' + d.scheme + '</span>' : '') + '</div>';
      });
      if (depDets.length > 4) html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#999;">+' + (depDets.length-4) + ' more</div>';
    }
    if (disDets.length) {
      html += '<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:#c62828;margin:6px 0 3px;">Disbursements</div>';
      disDets.slice(0,3).forEach(function(d) {
        html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#666;padding:2px 0;border-bottom:1px dotted #eee;">' +
          (d.loanAcNo||'') + ' · ' + (d.name||'').substring(0,18) + ' · ₹' + (parseFloat(d.amount)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN') + '</div>';
      });
    }
    if (repDets.length) {
      html += '<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:#2e7d32;margin:6px 0 3px;">Repayments</div>';
      repDets.slice(0,3).forEach(function(d) {
        html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:#666;padding:2px 0;border-bottom:1px dotted #eee;">' +
          (d.loanAcNo||'') + ' · ₹' + (parseFloat(d.paid)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN') +
          (d.interest ? ' +Int ₹' + (parseFloat(d.interest)||0).toLocaleString('en-IN') : '') + '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
  });
  html += '</div></div>';
  return html;
}

// ── Print ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function printDailyReport() {
  var content = document.getElementById('dailyReportPrintArea');
  if (!content) return;
  var el = document.getElementById('rptPanelTotal');
  if (el) el.style.display = 'block';
  var w = window.open('', '_blank');
  w.document.write(
    '<html><head><title>Daily Report</title>' +
    '<style>body{font-family:Arial,sans-serif;margin:20px;color:#2c3e50;font-size:12px;}' +
    '.no-print{display:none!important;}' +
    'table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;}' +
    'th,td{border:1px solid #ddd;padding:6px 8px;}' +
    '</style></head><body>' + content.innerHTML + '</body></html>'
  );
  w.document.close();
  w.focus();
  setTimeout(function(){ w.print(); w.close(); }, 600);
}

// ── Other Entry Modal ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function showOtherEntryModal() {
  var existing = document.getElementById('otherEntryModal');
  if (existing) existing.remove();
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      var rHeads = (res && res.receiptHeads) ? res.receiptHeads : ['Other Receipt'];
      var pHeads = (res && res.paymentHeads) ? res.paymentHeads : ['Other Payment'];
      var rOptions = rHeads.map(function(h){ return '<option value="'+h+'">'+h+'</option>'; }).join('');
      var pOptions = pHeads.map(function(h){ return '<option value="'+h+'">'+h+'</option>'; }).join('');
      var modal = document.createElement('div');
      modal.id = 'otherEntryModal';
      modal.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;top:0;left:0;width:100%;height:100%;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.65);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;z-index:9999;padding:20px;';
      modal.innerHTML =
        '<div style="background:white;border-radius:16px;padding:28px;max-width:440px;width:100%;max-height:90vh;overflow-y:auto;">' +
          '<h3 style="color:#2c3e50;margin:0 0 20px 0;text-align:center;">➕ Add Other Entry</h3>' +
          '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-bottom:18px;">' +
            '<button id="oeTypeReceipt" onclick="setOtherEntryType(\'RECEIPT\')" style="flex:1;padding:10px;background:#27ae60;color:white;border:none;border-radius:8px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;">📥 Receipt</button>' +
            '<button id="oeTypePayment" onclick="setOtherEntryType(\'PAYMENT\')" style="flex:1;padding:10px;background:#ecf0f1;color:#2c3e50;border:none;border-radius:8px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;">📤 Payment</button>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<input type="hidden" id="oeType" value="RECEIPT">' +
          '<label style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:#333;">Head / Category *</label>' +
          '<select id="oeHead" style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:2px solid #e0e0e0;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;margin:6px 0 14px;box-sizing:border-box;">' +
            '<optgroup label="📥 Receipt Heads" id="oeReceiptGroup">' + rOptions + '</optgroup>' +
            '<optgroup label="📤 Payment Heads" id="oePaymentGroup" style="display:none">' + pOptions + '</optgroup>' +
          '</select>' +
          '<label style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:#333;">Amount (₹) *</label>' +
          '<input type="number" id="oeAmount" placeholder="e.g. 500" min="1" style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:2px solid #e0e0e0;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;margin:6px 0 14px;box-sizing:border-box;">' +
          '<label style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:#333;">Remarks</label>' +
          '<input type="text" id="oeRemarks" placeholder="Optional" style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:2px solid #e0e0e0;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;margin:6px 0 14px;box-sizing:border-box;">' +
          '<label style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:#333;">Date *</label>' +
          '<input type="date" id="oeDate" style="width:100%;padding:10px;border:2px solid #e0e0e0;border-radius:8px;font-size:14px;margin:6px 0 18px;box-sizing:border-box;">' +
          '<div id="oeMsg" style="display:none;padding:10px;border-radius:8px;margin-bottom:12px;font-size:13px;"></div>' +
          '<div style="display:flex;gap:10px;">' +
            '<button onclick="document.getElementById(\'otherEntryModal\').remove()" style="flex:1;padding:12px;background:#ecf0f1;border:none;border-radius:8px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;color:#2c3e50;">Cancel</button>' +
            '<button onclick="submitOtherEntry()" id="oeSubmitBtn" style="flex:1;padding:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#8e44ad,#9b59b6);color:white;border:none;border-radius:8px;font-weight:bold;cursor:pointer;">Save Entry</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
      document.body.appendChild(modal);
      // ✅ FIX: Day begin date se lock karo
var dayDate = sessionStorage.getItem('activeDayDate') || '';
var today   = new Date();
var todayStr = today.getFullYear() + '-' + String(today.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0') + '-' + String(today.getDate()).padStart(2,'0');
var lockDate = dayDate || todayStr;
var dateEl = document.getElementById('oeDate');
dateEl.value    = lockDate;
dateEl.readOnly = true;
dateEl.style.background = '#f0f4ff';
dateEl.style.color      = '#1a237e';
dateEl.style.fontWeight = 'bold';
dateEl.title = '📅 Sirf Day Begin date allowed: ' + lockDate;
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(){ alert('❌ Could not load entry heads. Try again.'); })
    .getOtherEntryHeads();
}

function setOtherEntryType(type) {
  document.getElementById('oeType').value = type;
  var rBtn = document.getElementById('oeTypeReceipt');
  var pBtn = document.getElementById('oeTypePayment');
  var rGrp = document.getElementById('oeReceiptGroup');
  var pGrp = document.getElementById('oePaymentGroup');
  if (type === 'RECEIPT') {
    rBtn.style.background='#27ae60'; rBtn.style.color='white';
    pBtn.style.background='#ecf0f1'; pBtn.style.color='#2c3e50';
    if(rGrp) rGrp.style.display=''; if(pGrp) pGrp.style.display='none';
  } else {
    pBtn.style.background='#e74c3c'; pBtn.style.color='white';
    rBtn.style.background='#ecf0f1'; rBtn.style.color='#2c3e50';
    if(rGrp) rGrp.style.display='none'; if(pGrp) pGrp.style.display='';
  }
}

function submitOtherEntry() {
  var type    = document.getElementById('oeType').value;
  var head    = document.getElementById('oeHead').value;
  var amount  = parseFloat(document.getElementById('oeAmount').value) || 0;
  var remarks = document.getElementById('oeRemarks').value.trim();
  var date    = document.getElementById('oeDate').value;
  var btn     = document.getElementById('oeSubmitBtn');
  if (!head)              { _oeMsg('❌ Head/category select karo', 'error'); return; }
  if (!amount||amount<=0) { _oeMsg('❌ Valid amount enter karo', 'error'); return; }
  if (!date)              { _oeMsg('❌ Date select karo', 'error'); return; }
  btn.disabled=true; btn.textContent='⏳ Saving...';
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(res) {
      btn.disabled=false; btn.textContent='Save Entry';
      if (res && res.success) {
        _oeMsg('✅ ' + res.message, 'success');
        setTimeout(function(){
          document.getElementById('otherEntryModal').remove();
          loadDailyReport(document.getElementById('dailyReportDate').value);
        }, 1500);
      } else {
        _oeMsg('❌ ' + (res ? res.message : 'Error'), 'error');
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err){ btn.disabled=false; btn.textContent='Save Entry'; _oeMsg('❌ '+err.message,'error'); })
    .saveOtherEntry(currentUserId, { type:type, head:head, amount:amount, remarks:remarks, date:date });
}

function _oeMsg(msg, type) {
  var d = document.getElementById('oeMsg');
  if (!d) return;
  d.textContent = msg;
  d.style.background = type==='success' ? '#d4edda' : '#f8d7da';
  d.style.color      = type==='success' ? '#155724' : '#721c24';
  d.style.display    = 'block';
}
function filterByStatus(status) {
  if (!status) { renderMemberRequests(allMemberRequests); return; }
  var filtered = allMemberRequests.filter(function(r){ return r.status === status; });
  renderMemberRequests(filtered);
}
</script>
